Important Foreign News

Formation of the New French Cabinet

Laval Also Serves as Foreign Minister

Tardieu Heads the Army

No Major Changes to the Previous Members

Reuter's, Paris, 13th – Due to the death of Minister of the Army Maginot and the resignation of Foreign Minister Briand, Laval intended to reorganize the national cabinet to address important conferences such as those on reparations and disarmament. He invited Herriot to take the position of Foreign Minister, but the Radical Socialist Party did not allow its leader Herriot to take office. As a result, Laval's cabinet collectively resigned on Tuesday. President Doumer then requested Laval to form a new cabinet. Laval immediately set about the task, making slight changes to the old cabinet members. Soon after, he drew up a list of cabinet members and submitted it to the President for review. Laval transferred Minister of Agriculture Tardieu to head the Army, and he himself took on the role of Foreign Minister, as a suitable candidate for this position was difficult to find at the moment. Laval, who had been serving as Minister of the Interior, now also heads the Foreign Ministry. Therefore, he appointed Chautemps to head the Ministry of the Interior, and Fould to head the Ministry of Agriculture in place of Tardieu. All other existing cabinet members remain unchanged. Thus, the cabinet was formed. Although it did not form a national government as desired by the public, pressing global issues such as reparations and disarmament urgently need to be addressed. Therefore, the opposition party is temporarily willing to support the government, pending the general election for the National Assembly. The Radical Socialist Party hopes to win a major victory in the general election in April, so it is unwilling to accept Laval's invitation to join the cabinet. However, on current important international issues, the Radical Socialist Party's views do not differ significantly from Laval's. Regarding Laval's domestic standing, the death of Maginot and the departure of Briand have both weakened Laval's position, as Maginot had the support of the right wing, and Briand was greatly supported by the left wing. Laval seems to be aware of this, so he stated that he has requested Briand to continue lending his influence and experience to the current government. It is expected that Briand will be a Minister without Portfolio and the permanent French representative to the League of Nations. The new government is scheduled to meet with the National Assembly on Tuesday.

The United States Will Not Participate in the Lausanne Reparations Conference

National, Washington, 13th – U.S. Secretary of State Stimson announced today that the United States will not send representatives to the international reparations conference. Although the United States has no direct relationship with reparations, its relationship with war debts is extremely significant. The decision of whether or not to participate in the Lausanne Conference has been uncertain for several weeks. Initially, Ogden and Deputy Secretary of the Treasury Mills expressed that the United States would only participate if the Lausanne Conference expanded its agenda to discuss global economic and financial issues. Recently, the voices in Europe demanding the cancellation of war debts and reparations have become increasingly louder, and opponents in the United States have also grown in number. It is likely that the U.S. government has therefore made a swift and clear statement. However, although the United States will not formally participate, it will still pay close attention to the Lausanne Conference due to its relationship with war debts.

The Situation of the International Disarmament Conference is Not Optimistic

Reuter's, Geneva, 14th – Although the Geneva Disarmament Conference is scheduled to open on February 2nd, according to today's news, the most important key to the disarmament issue may not be mentioned before Easter. The first six weeks after the opening will mostly be spent on preliminary discussions, and then the conference will adjourn. By April, the International Labour Conference may need to open, and after the Labour Conference, France and Germany will need to hold parliamentary elections. All of these factors may prevent the Disarmament Conference from immediately resuming after the Easter holiday. If so, a long period of adjournment will be unavoidable. The number of representatives attending may not be as large as expected, as countries are bound to greatly reduce their participating representatives due to economic difficulties.

British Commission to India

Proceeding with the Round Table Conference Process

Bombay Bans Anti-British Propaganda

Reuter's, London, 14th – The British members of the three commissions to India to implement the work of the Round Table Conference set off for Bombay today, not deterred by the non-violent resistance movement within India. The British government has decided to ignore the activities of the All-India Congress and continue with the procedures outlined in the Round Table Conference. These three commissions include: ㈠ An Assessment of Financial Standing, chaired by Peel, will assess the financial standing of the central and provincial governments after the reforms. ㈠ The Handling of Suffrage Issues, chaired by Lothian, will establish new mechanisms for the public participation of people in various provinces and important regions. ㈠ The Unification of Financial Relations, chaired by Davidson, will unify the financial relations between the Indian government and several Indian princely states. Representatives of all parties from the previous Round Table Conference, except for members of the All-India Congress, will consult with the three commissions in India to plan its progress. In addition, there is a Working Committee, whose members are appointed by British Prime Minister MacDonald. The British government strongly supports the principles of an all-India federation and a responsible central government, but there must be certain reservations and guarantees for the time being. These three commissions will carry out their investigations in order to achieve this goal. They will have close contact with the British government.

Reuter's, London, 13th – The blue book on the minutes of the Federal Structure and Minorities Committees of the Indian Round Table Conference was published today. It has 600 pages, with over one million words, and sells for twenty-five shillings. The book is 13 inches long, 8 inches wide, and over an inch thick.

Havas, Bombay, 13th – The Bombay provincial government recently notified newspaper publishers that any news that encourages the non-violent resistance movement will be subject to criminal penalties if published by newspapers. The maximum penalty can be up to two years in prison.

U.S. Treasury Secretary Mellon Accused of Using Public Office for Private Gain

Bittman Impeaches Mellon Before the House

Demonstrates the Spirit of a Rule of Law Nation

National, Washington, 13th – U.S. Congressman Bittman's impeachment case against Treasury Secretary Mellon was publicly heard by the House today, with Bittman presenting evidence. If the House deems the evidence sufficient in the future, it will pass the case and impeach Mellon. According to Bittman, he is not accusing Mellon of corruption but of violating the law and oath of office by continuing to run private businesses since becoming the head of the Treasury Department in 1921, for personal gain. He cited several instances over the years of Mellon favoring private businesses as evidence.

New Chinese Envoy to Germany Presents Credentials

National, Berlin, 14th – The newly appointed Chinese Envoy to Germany, Liu Wentao, met with the German President today to present his credentials. After the formal ceremony, the German President spoke with Envoy Liu for a long time. In his address, Liu expressed the friendly relations between China and Germany, stating that he would do his best to enhance the economic and cultural cooperation between the two countries. President Hindenburg replied that Germany has gained greatly from the East and hopes that there will be closer cooperation between the East and West in the future.

Minseito Party Establishes New Policies

Japanese Parliament Likely to be Dissolved

Total National Debt Reaches 6 Billion Yuan

Dentsu, Tokyo, 14th – The declaration and new policies to be issued by the Minseito Party at the party congress on the 20th have been largely determined by a special committee as follows: "Economic and Financial Policies"

㈠ Realize the gold standard system, ㈡ Improve industrial organization based on state control, ㈢ Establish a tariff policy aimed at protecting and promoting domestic industries, ㈣ Improve the financial system, especially public finance, "Rural Relief Measures" ㈠ Consolidate the burdens of rural areas, ㈡ Rationalize fertilizer distribution, ㈢ Stabilize cocoon silk and rice prices, "Social Policy" ㈠ Build a new economic policy based on cooperation between labor and management, ㈡ Formulate various social legislations that adapt to the new society, "Diplomatic Issues" ㈠ Fundamentally resolve various pending issues with China, ㈡ Promote the resolution of international issues through the League of Nations system. Japan News Agency, Tokyo, 14th – The dissolution of the 60th Parliament has been confirmed. However, the government is extremely pessimistic because income has decreased greatly, and there is a huge surplus budget. Although 17 million yuan was repaid in December last year, there are still more than 6 billion yuan due to the issuance of railway bonds and treasury bonds.

Woman Elected to Senate

First in American History

Reuter's, Washington, 13th – Mrs. Carraway was elected today in the Arkansas Democratic primary for Senate. This is the first time in history that a woman has been elected as a member of the U.S. Senate.

Ex-German Emperor Suffers from Tracheitis

His Sister, Sophia, Passes Away

National, Doorn, Netherlands, 13th – Ex-German Emperor Wilhelm, aged 73, recently caught a cold after working outdoors. After recovering from the cold, he is now suffering from tracheitis and has been bedridden for days. Many people have visited to inquire about his health.

Havas, Frankfurt, 13th – The ex-German Emperor's sister, former Greek Queen Sophia, who had been seriously ill and treated at a private hospital here for several weeks, passed away this evening.

Reuter's, Frankfurt, 13th – Former Greek Queen Sophia passed away here today at the age of 62. Sophia was the granddaughter of British Queen Victoria. Her father was German Emperor Wilhelm III, and she was the sister of the ex-German Emperor. At the age of 19, she married Greek Crown Prince Constantine. In 1913, Constantine ascended the Greek throne. In 1922, he was forced to cede the throne to his son George II. A few months later, George was expelled, and Greece changed to a democratic system. Queen Sophia then took refuge in Italy. Last year, she went to Frankfurt, Germany, for medical treatment, but she never recovered.

Krupp Steel Factory in Germany Closes

Over Four Thousand Workers Lose Jobs

Reuter's, Berlin, 14th – The Krupp Company's Eisen steel factory closed today due to a lack of orders, causing more than four thousand workers to be unemployed. This is the third largest factory closure in Germany since December 21st. Company officials said they would try to reopen the factory, but they could not say when it would be possible to resume work.

Tokyo Tram Workers Resume Work

Japan News Agency, Tokyo, 14th – Five hundred and fifty employees of the Tokyo City Tram Hiroo depot suddenly went on strike yesterday. By 5 p.m., they cooperated with the employees of the Kinshibori depot. However, the headquarters of the striking group was controlled by the leftist Zenkyo group, so there was no control. The executives of the Tokyo Transportation Labor Union met with the city tram bureau officials three times and decided to entrust the director of the tram bureau, Tateishi, to resolve the case. As a result, the Hiroo depot employees started working at 9 a.m., and the Kinshibori depot employees started working at 10:40 a.m.

Important News

Major Riot by Japanese in Qingdao

Burning of the City Party Headquarters and the Min Guo Daily Newspaper Office

Jinan Correspondence, The Min Guo Daily Newspaper Office on Zhongshan Road, Qingdao, suddenly had two Japanese men, each holding a glass bottle, throw them into the furnace downstairs at 9:15 a.m. on the 11th. They turned and ran away. As soon as they ran out, there was a loud explosion. Fortunately, no one was injured at the time. The newspaper office immediately sounded the alarm and chased after them. Unexpectedly, the Japanese men took out pistols and shot at the pursuing police, firing as they ran until they reached the Japanese Resident Group Department on Hunan Road. Because the Japanese side was intentionally provoking, the police did not pursue them further. That evening, the municipal government lodged a protest with the Japanese Consul, but the Japanese Consul did not reply. Unexpectedly, on the 12th, the situation escalated. At around 9 a.m., many Japanese men, carrying flammable materials, set fire to the Min Guo Daily, surrounded the building, and prevented anyone from putting out the fire. They also opened fire, preventing our fire department from approaching to extinguish the fire, and letting it burn. At 2 p.m., all Japanese residents in the city held a general meeting at the Resident Group Department. At 2 p.m., they set off in formation, shouting "Long live the Japanese Empire!" all the way until they reached the Qingdao City Party Headquarters on Taiping Road. They surrounded the party headquarters and expelled all personnel. At 9 p.m., they set fire to the building. After the City Party Headquarters caught fire, the Japanese were elated, shouting and jumping wildly, and firing guns as a show of force, still not allowing our fire department to approach to extinguish the fire. At the same time, the Japanese warships anchored in the front sea used searchlights to illuminate the city, shining brightly, further fueling the flames. As a result, both the City Party Headquarters and the Min Guo Daily Newspaper Office were completely reduced to ashes. All streets in the city are now closed to pedestrians, and the police have mostly fled. The situation is serious, and people are panicking, feeling that the end is near. (Evening of the 12th)

Complete Change of Personnel in Shandong's National Tax Agencies

Jinan Correspondence, All national tax agencies in Shandong are now being taken over by Han Fuju, who has replaced all personnel. Chai Chunlin (former director of the Shandong Local Official Property Clearance Office) has been appointed to the Salt Affairs Inspection Office, and Tian Lianzhong (former Linqing Customs Supervisor and Director of the Provincial Government General Affairs Office) has been appointed to the Nitrate and Sulfur Bureau. Both took office today. Chen Weixin (former mayor of Jinan City) has been appointed to the Consolidated Tax Collection Office and also took office today. Zhao Guangpei (Chief of the General Headquarters Staff Office) has been appointed as Deputy Commissioner of Salt Transport in Qingdao. Zhao is currently in Beiping and will go to Qingdao to take office upon his return from Beiping. Qin Chao-wu (Director of the 21st Division's Office in Jinan) has been appointed as Deputy Commissioner of Salt Transport in Yantai and will go to take office in the next few days. Jiao Zilong has been newly appointed to the Anti-Smuggling Brigade of the Salt Affairs Inspection Office and took office today. Someone has also been appointed to the Shandong Provincial Mining Tax Collection Office, and there are reports that he has already taken office, but the name is unknown. According to the new Salt Transport Commissioner Li Wuchen, the local takeover of the salt affairs agencies does not affect foreign debts. After this, salt tax revenue will be allocated to foreign debts first, and the remainder will be retained for the province's military expenses.

Also, Chen Weixin, Director of the Shandong Inspection Office of the Lu-Yu Consolidated Tax Bureau, stated after taking office today that the province's takeover of the national tax agencies was due to the central government's failure to pay Shandong's military expenses for three months. A special request was made to temporarily take over the agencies to make up for the shortfall. Other provinces have already taken over the national tax agencies, and this province has been the latest to take over. The Consolidated Tax Bureau manages flour, cotton yarn, cigarettes, and matches. However, according to the office's past practice, the officers and staff would send the tax revenue to the Central Bank on a regular basis, and the Central Bank would send a list at the end of the month to the office, which would then forward it to the Ministry of Finance. It was just an empty forwarding agency. It is said that the office's tax revenue can reach tens of thousands of yuan per month. (12th)

The Issue of Reorganization of Liu Guitang's Troops

Liu Requests Military Uniforms First

And Waiting for Yin's Troops to Open Gaotang

Jinan Correspondence, After Liu Guitang, Yin Shigui, and Guo Wensheng's (i.e., Guo Ma Feng) troops arrived at Da Wen Kou from Da Bianqiao, they wanted to go on foot to Gaotang after being reorganized at Da Wen Kou. However, Shandong Governor Han Fuju still ordered them to take a car to Gaotang first, and then send someone to reorganize them. Yesterday, Han sent a telegram to Liu explaining everything, and also sent Adjutant Director Meng Guangshan, together with Liu Guitang's representative Xia Ziming, and Zhang Futian, the original introducer from the Shandong Native Place Association in Tianjin, to Da Wen Kou to meet Liu and convey Han's intentions. Meng Guangshan also prepared vehicles in Da Wen Kou to prepare for transportation. Meng, Xia, and Zhang took a car from Jinan at 9:00 a.m. this morning (12th) and arrived at Da Wen Kou at 1:00 p.m. At that time, Liu Guitang's troops were there to greet them. Although they were all in plain clothes, their spirits were very good. Zhang Yuru, the president of the Da Wen Kou Chamber of Commerce, also came to the station to welcome them. They entered the town together. Slogans were posted all along the way, reading "Welcome Military Commander Liu" and "Welcome Military Commander Liu, who defeated the Japanese at Sai Ma Zhan Shan." Xia and others went directly to the Yuelai Store, because Liu Guitang's headquarters was located there. When they arrived at the Yuelai Store, Liu personally went out on horseback to patrol the streets to prevent his subordinates from acting out of line. Xia and others waited temporarily. After a short while, Liu returned and greeted each other. After sitting down, they talked. Liu spoke frankly and did not lose the true colors of a bandit. Xia and Zhang first reported on the situation in Jinan and Governor Han's hope that he would take a car to Gaotang first for reorganization. Liu replied that his surrender this time was because he was from Shandong. He had been a military commander and division commander and had led troops for more than ten years. Out of love for his hometown, he surrendered. He was forty years old. Four or five years ago, he heard that there were runners in the South Mountain with a total of 6,000 guns. The first time he was taken over by Zhang Jingyao and disarmed in Hunan. The second time he was taken over by Wu Yuyu and disarmed in the old nest, with 3,000 guns disarmed, leaving only 1,000 guns. The third time he was taken over by Sun Meiyao, and disarmed by Wu Ziming of the Fifth Division, leaving only 1,000 guns. The fourth time he was taken over and disarmed by Xu Kun. He went to Henan and served as a vanguard army during the Northern Expedition, making great contributions to defeating Zhang Zongchang. When he was in Henan, he guarded Yu Prefecture and claimed that he had made no mistakes. Even if he had made mistakes, he should have been remembered for his past achievements, but he was still resolved. His surrender this time was the fifth time. He was very grateful to Governor Han and hated that he could not open his heart for people to see. He decided to repay Governor Han. When he was in the mountains, the Japanese went to buy him to disrupt Jiaodong, but he refused. When he was in Rizhao, the Japanese came twice, willing to help with guns and money, to make him disrupt the area. He would rather go begging than be used by the Japanese, etc.

It is heard that Liu had two requests: 1. Send military uniforms first, then open Gaotang. 2. Wait for Yin Shigui's troops to open Gaotang together. He planned to ask Xia Ziming to go to Teng County from Da Wen Kou on the 13th to pull Yin Shigui's troops. Yin's troops have more than 2,000 guns in the mountains. Liu said that he would never abandon them. Yin's troops also wanted to walk to Da Wen Kou and did not want to take a car. Liu also said that his troops had 10,000 people, and 10,000 sets of military uniforms would only cost 30,000 yuan, while disrupting a village would cause greater losses. Finally, Liu also said that if 20,000 people were used to solve his troops, it would be better to use these 30,000 people to fight the Japanese. He believed that this time's surrender would completely pull out all the large and small bandits to serve the country, so that the 40-year banditry in southern Shandong would be completely suppressed, which would be a better strategy, etc. It is heard that Xia and others immediately reported to Han by telegram Liu's request for military uniforms first and then open Gaotang, and wait for Yin Shigui to go together, asking for instructions on how to handle it. The armored car from Beiping opened Da Wen Kou from Jinan at 3:00 p.m. today.

Regarding the telegrams between Gu Liangmin, Liu Shuxiang, and Han Fuju regarding the reorganization of Liu Guitang and Guo's troops, the appendix is as follows: 1. This is the biggest reason why brother can't help but doubt them. I hope my brother will pay special attention, this reply, Han Fuju Wen Shen Yin Can,

Huang Xiansheng Reports on the Anti-Japanese War Efforts of the Volunteer Army Outside the Pass

The Anti-Japanese Association of Northeastern People in Beiping held a welcome meeting at the Fengtian Guildhall at 1:30 PM on the 11th, attended by over fifty people to welcome Huang Xiansheng, the Commissioner of Liaoning Police, who had returned from Shenyang. The meeting was chaired by Wang Huayi, the president of the association. After the opening remarks by the chairman, Huang Xiansheng reported on the volunteer army's battle with the Japanese army outside the pass. Finally, the chairman gave a thank-you speech, and the meeting adjourned at 2:30 PM. The following is a transcript of Huang Xiansheng's report:

Before reporting on the fourteen days of fighting between the volunteer army and the Japanese army, I would like to first explain the origins of the volunteer army. Most people regard the volunteer army as bandits, but before the September 18th Incident, the total number of bandits in the province was only about 1,800. After the incident, volunteer armies sprang up everywhere, which proves that the volunteer army is not made up of bandits. Before the Anti-Japanese Association took the lead, the volunteer army may have had some irregularities, and their food and clothing were not systematically arranged, so they raised funds everywhere, which the Japanese then used to spread propaganda about them being bandits. In fact, the volunteer army is a group of ordinary people in the Eastern Provinces who have risen up to defend themselves. These untrained ordinary people are using 19th-century weapons to resist a powerful country with modern weaponry. Therefore, we should study the organization and guidance of the volunteer army based on the current situation in order to confront the enemy and recover the lost territory.

The first time the Japanese army attacked Jinzhou, the troops passed through Xinmin. Due to the inconvenience of transportation at the time, it was agreed that when the Japanese army passed through Xinmin, the volunteer army would rise up and fight them. After the Japanese army passed Xinmin, the volunteer army occupied Juluhe and advanced to Huanggu Tun. Both sides suffered enormous losses in the battle.

The original plan of the Japanese army was to attack Jinzhou with a brigade, but they realized the danger of attacking along a single route, so the Japanese army changed their plan. Originally, the Tamon Division was to attack Heilongjiang, and a brigade transferred from Hokkaido was to attack Jinzhou. After the change of plan, three brigades from Hokkaido were transferred to attack Heilongjiang, the Tamon Division attacked Jinzhou, and two brigades were transferred from Korea to attack Heilongjiang.

On December 20th, the Japanese army launched an offensive from Xingcheng. At Menling, they began to clash with the 14th Detachment of the Second Route of our Volunteer Army. The Japanese side had four to five hundred cavalrymen, while our side had even more cavalrymen. The Second and Fourth Routes concentrated their forces in Shaling to fight, and the Japanese army was unable to advance. Later, the Japanese army set out for Tianzhuangtai, and two battalions of our 19th Brigade and one battalion of the Coastal Defense Brigade were trapped. The two battalions of the 19th Brigade escaped, but the Coastal Defense Brigade was never able to retreat. Later, the volunteer army went to their aid and fought fiercely for two days and two nights before they were able to lift the siege. Both sides suffered heavy casualties. The volunteer army captured eleven cannons (including six Taisho mountain guns and five new-style cannons), captured forty-eight prisoners, and seized two hundred and seventy-three rifles. Later, more than eighty Japanese soldiers were surrounded by our army, but the local business community compromised with the Japanese army and fought against us, which allowed the Japanese army to break the siege.

On the 29th, the 19th Brigade of Panshan completely withdrew without notifying the volunteer army, which led to the Japanese occupation. Later, the volunteer army recaptured it. At that time, there were more than four hundred wounded volunteer soldiers in Tianzhuangtai, Dakua, and Shaling, and the hospitals and other places were not prepared. Those with minor injuries were given fifty silver dollars each and sent to neighboring villages, and over a hundred people were transported to Jinzhou to prevent them from being secretly attacked by the enemy.

On the 30th, contact began at Dagushan. At that time, each volunteer soldier had one hundred and fifty bullets, but by the time they reached the north bank of the Daling River, each soldier only had thirty or forty bullets. By the 1st, bullets could not be transported, and order along the stations was also disrupted, so by the morning of the 2nd, the source of bullets had been cut off. However, the Second Detachment of our Volunteer Army fought very well, surrounding forty Japanese soldiers in a village. More than two hundred volunteer soldiers rode horses to Jinzhou to collect bullets, but due to the lack of bullets, they were unable to do so. At that time, the officer burst into tears and gave all the bullets in his possession to them to take away.

On the morning of the 2nd, when the Japanese army intended to attack Jinzhou, all the troops in Jinzhou were mobilized and a section of the railway was destroyed. On the evening of the 3rd, the personnel withdrew from Jinxi. This war lasted for fourteen days, and a total of eleven cannons and over four hundred and eighty rifles were obtained. The purpose of coming to Beiping this time is to plan future combat strategies, the source of bullets, and the compensation for the casualties.

I can also briefly report on the enemy's plans. After the Japanese army presses the Liaoxi army into the pass, they plan to have Zhang Xiantao's army occupy Rehe. On the 4th, they will mobilize the Tamon army to clear our army in Liaodong, and then they will use their entire force to clear our army in Jilin and Heilongjiang. For the civilians, they will confiscate weapons and eliminate the strength of the people. Economically, they plan to use all the Feng Piao notes of the official silver bank to purchase grain and produce from the people, and then issue Municipal Bank notes "kind" and declare Feng Piao notes invalid in order to cut off the people's economy.

The National Government Persuades Li Mingzhong to Stay

Hankou Correspondence: Li Mingzhong, the Pacification Commissioner of the Henan-Hubei-Anhui Border Region and concurrently the Commander-in-Chief of the Eastern Hubei Bandit Suppression, had previously resigned from the National Government due to illness and went to Huangpi to await orders. After receiving the telegram, the National Government, recognizing Li's remarkable achievements in pacifying the local area, replied on the 12th to persuade him to stay. At the same time, Chief of Staff Zhu Peide and Minister of Military Affairs He Yingqin also replied, expressing their concern for his illness and urging him to continue to shoulder the heavy responsibility at a time of national crisis, to quell internal disturbances and resist foreign aggression, and to work together for the country.

Li went to Huangpi on the 11th and returned to Hankou on the 12th. After reading the two telegrams, he reportedly cancelled his resignation. He will continue to lead his troops to suppress bandits. Although the bandit leader, Kuang, has retreated from Huang'an, he has not suffered any real losses. It is reported that the Central Government has decided to order the troops stationed in the three provinces of Henan, Anhui, and Hubei to carry out a thorough joint suppression. The Eastern Hubei front will be under the command of Li, with the 30th, 31st, 33rd, 13th, and part of the 48th Divisions under his command. The Southern Henan front will be under the command of Zhang Fang, with the 11th, 45th, 58th, 75th, 76th, and 20th Divisions under his command. The Western Anhui front will be under the command of Yue Shengxuan, with the 46th, 55th, one brigade of the 57th Division, and the Zheng and Song brigades under his command. All of these forces will be under the direct command of Liu Zhi, the Pacification Commissioner stationed in Henan. The total bandit suppression force is about thirteen divisions, which should be enough to wipe them out in one fell swoop. (January 13th)

Local Correspondence

Fengxian

Hubei Refugees Cause Great Disturbance: Yesterday, over five hundred refugees from Huangmei County, Hubei, arrived in the area from Songjiang. As they passed through Zhugang, it was already late at night. The refugees, using the excuse of borrowing stoves to cook, entered people's homes and caused great disturbances. At the same time, they swarmed into the residence of Xue Zhaoqian, a wealthy household in the area, and robbed him of gold, silver, jewelry, cloth, food, and other items worth several hundred dollars. After receiving the report today, the county's Public Security Bureau immediately sent police to drive them away to prevent future troubles.

Wrongful Accusation of Communist Party Membership Leads to Six-Month Sentence: Gu Genlou, a villager from Sanjiao Yang Township in the Second District, was sentenced to six months in prison for falsely accusing his uncle, Gu Meisheng, and his maternal uncle, Chen Chunlin, of being communists because he had been unable to borrow money from them. The case was initially investigated by the Fourth Brigade of the Anti-Smuggling Police stationed there and sent to the county government. After investigation, they were found to be innocent and were released on bail. At the same time, Gu Genlou was sentenced to six months in prison for false accusation as a warning. However, Gu appealed to the High Court after the sentence was pronounced in court, expressing his dissatisfaction. After repeated trials, the court found no reason to overturn the original verdict. Therefore, the court yesterday (the 13th) sent the accused back to the original trial court for enforcement.

Suzhou

Financial Panic Occurs in Suzhou: Recently, rumors have been circulating about the suspension of interest payments on government bonds. The Suzhou money market has suddenly become tense. On the 13th, the money market closed at 9:30 PM, with the exchange rate rising to 7 fen 3 li 6 hao per tael of silver. Yesterday (the 14th), the market had not yet opened by 7:00 PM, and the situation was very panic-stricken.

The County Chamber of Commerce and the three financial groups of the money industry and the banking industry sent urgent telegrams to the National Government's Executive Yuan, the Ministry of Finance, and the Treasury Bond Fund Management Committee yesterday (the 14th), stating that "At this time, when the end of the year is approaching, if the suspension of payments is true, the national financial situation will be in dire straits, and how can businesses in various places be spared? Our association and others are deeply concerned and cannot remain silent. We humbly request that you consider public opinion and make a clear statement that the rumor of suspending the payment of principal and interest on bonds will never be realized. We also request that all provinces not withhold tax revenues in order to secure the central government and maintain public confidence."

Gu Enjin's Embezzlement Case Appeals Sentencing: Gu Enjin, the former manager of the Changshu branch of the Bank of Communications, embezzled over 280,000 yuan of the bank's funds and fled to Suzhou. He was arrested and handed over to the local court, which sentenced him to six months in prison and a fine of 1,000 yuan. Gu appealed to the High Court, dissatisfied with the original verdict. Yesterday (the 14th), the court announced its verdict, overturning the original sentence. Gu Enjin was sentenced to three years in prison and fined 1,500 yuan for embezzlement.

Wuxi

Suzhou Robbery Suspects Arrested in Wuxi: Xun Gongting, the patrol officer of the First Police Station of the Third Branch of the Public Security Bureau at the Shangpailou in the South Gate of this county, led police officers to seize a stolen boat in front of the Fengfu Silk Factory under the nearby Ta Bridge the day before yesterday. Three robbers, Chen Wenxi, Jiang Er, and Jiang Minshi, were arrested. After being brought to the police station for strict interrogation, Chen and the others confessed that they had previously robbed the home of Qian Songyao, a resident of No. 28 Enpo Lane in Suzhou City. Director Hua of the Public Security Bureau immediately telegraphed the Suzhou Public Security Bureau, requesting that they send personnel with documents to Wuxi to arrest and bring them to justice.

Joint Defense Measures on the Border of Jiangsu and Zhejiang: The governments of Jiangsu and Zhejiang provinces have recently been concerned about the bandits of Taihu Lake, who frequently cause trouble. In order to eliminate bandits and stabilize the border area, they have ordered the water police of Jiangsu and Zhejiang provinces to conduct joint patrols on a regular basis and have formulated the following permanent joint defense measures for the Jiangsu-Zhejiang border:

1. Fifteen counties, including Wujiang, Wuxian, Songjiang, Qingpu, Kunshan, Wuxi, Wujin, Yixing in Jiangsu, and Changxing, Tongxiang, Chongde, Jiaxing, Pinghu, and Jiashan in Zhejiang, will be designated as permanent joint defense areas.

2. The locations of the army, navy, and police stationed within the defense area will be reported by the senior officers of each side once a month. Any changes will be reported immediately.

3. The army, navy, and police stationed within the defense area should closely investigate the bandits within the defense area, clearly identifying the number of personnel, weapons, and bases, and reporting them to each other for joint suppression.

4. In the event of bandit activity within the area, all army, navy, and police, regardless of where it occurs or which jurisdiction it belongs to, must immediately report to each other and cooperate in the suppression, without dividing the border between provinces and counties or the chain of command, which would cause obstruction. Violators will be punished for dereliction of duty.

5. If bandits appear within the defense area, the army, navy, and police must track them down and eliminate them.

6. The passwords, signals, and flags used by the army, navy, and police in the defense area when suppressing bandits will be carefully determined by the senior officers of the two provinces and reported to each other for implementation.

Jiangyin

Two Robbery Cases Occur in the Suburbs: Three bandits suddenly came to the Silkworm Seed Improvement Center outside the West Gate, entered and robbed them, but since there was no silver, they forcibly took several pieces of clothing and left. Also, the home of Duan Apei in Xieyuan Township outside the South Gate was visited by more than ten bandits at eleven o'clock the night before last. They entered and robbed him. Apei had died many years ago, and his wife was sleeping alone at home. She was first raped by the bandits and then wrapped in a sheet, intending to kidnap her. Fearing that she would make noise, they stabbed her in the face with a knife and robbed her of more than two hundred silver dollars. Duan's wife was abandoned in a wheat field halfway there.

The Sixth District Chief is Accused of Dismissal: Cao Zongduo, the chief of the Sixth District, has been in office for more than a year since being transferred from the Eighth District. Recently, he was accused by the people of the district on eleven counts, and they jointly accused him to the Department of Civil Affairs, the county government, and the party headquarters, and sent Huang Zhong to the Western Township to investigate secretly. The county party headquarters resolved at its regular meeting on the 12th to send a letter to the county to dismiss Cao.

Zhenjiang

Butcher Shop Owner Illegally Sells Military Supplies: Ma Laogen, a butcher shop owner in Wufengkou, Zhenjiang, was illegally transporting military supplies to supply bandits. After being discovered, it was secretly reported to the Ningzhen Pacification Sub-district Command, which immediately sent personnel to investigate and confirmed the facts of the illegal sale. It then dispatched dozens of plainclothes detectives to search the area and seized the illegal firearms dealer Ma Laogen (also known as Mingyu), Xie Gongzhen, and six other accomplices, along with several guns, and brought them back to Zhenjiang for interrogation.

Supervisory Yuan Thoroughly Investigates Corruption Case on the Beijing-Hangzhou Road: The case of the Jiangsu Provincial Department of Construction's Beijing-Hangzhou Road Project, involving the falsification of reports and embezzlement of large sums of money, has been pending for a long time since it was transferred to the Zhenjiang Court for investigation. Now, the National Government's Supervisory Yuan, based on the report of the Jiangsu Provincial Party Department, has specially appointed three auditors from the Audit Department, Yin Gongwu, Wang Qichang, and Shao Chuanxin, to come to the province yesterday to investigate. They have already obtained case files from the Provincial Party Department, the Provincial Government, and the Zhenjiang Local Court. It is hoped that this large-scale corruption case will soon be brought to light.

Huge Amount of Opium Transported by Ship: At around 1:00 AM yesterday morning, the Osaka Company's Wuchang ship from Hankou passed through Zhenjiang. Zhang Guangyou reported from Hankou that there were forty-eight loads of opium being transported to Shanghai. Zhang then reported to the 121st Brigade of the 61st Division stationed in Zhenjiang. Brigade Commander Zhang Li sent a team to board the ship and search it. They found a large quantity of opium, totaling twelve Western flour sacks and two hemp sacks, all filled with opium, weighing approximately 13,000 taels. The opium was immediately unloaded and transported ashore. The ship was delayed as a result and did not depart for Shanghai until after 4:00 AM.

Yangzhou

The Mianbing Industry's Business Tax is Not Allowed to be Exempted: The Jiangdu Mianbing Industry representatives, Gao Jin and others, jointly submitted a request to the Chamber of Commerce, requesting exemption from business tax. Director Shu of the Department of Finance, based on the telegram from the County Chamber of Commerce, presented the previous reasons and requested review. He specially ordered the County Chamber of Commerce, stating that the pastry industry listed in the tax rate table for the sales industry refers to all kinds of pastries. If the annual turnover is over 1,000 yuan, it should be taxed accordingly. If it is less than the specified amount, it will not be taxed. Chairman Wang of the Chamber of Commerce yesterday (the 12th) forwarded the order to the tax collector Hui Bingwen to collect taxes in accordance with the regulations and informed the industry representatives to comply.

Two Robbery Cases Occur Consecutively in Yizheng Town: The home of Li Zhaozhu, a villager in Yiling Town, was suddenly visited by eight or nine bandits armed with short guns the night before (the 9th). They broke into the house and looted extensively, stealing clothes and other items. At the same time, the home of Jiang Zhihuai near the town was also visited by more than ten bandits who entered and tied Zhihuai's elderly father, Jiang Litan, to the stove. They first used fire to interrogate him, then stripped off his clothes.

Qingjiang

Bandits Murder the Victim: Li Shichen, a farmer in Touxiang Erzha, Huaiyin, was extremely poor and had nothing hidden in his home. At 11:00 PM on the 8th, more than ten bandits suddenly came and tied up Shichen. Shichen's wife, Zhang, saw her husband being carried away by the bandits and followed behind, crying for help. After walking half a mile, the bandits shot Shichen to death and strangled his neck with a rope. By the time Li Zhang arrived, Shichen had died and could not be saved. On the 9th, Li Zhang came to the county government to report the case and request that the criminals be arrested and brought to justice.

Jiangsu Education Director Zhou Fo Hai Sworn into Office

Willing to "Work Hard and Be Unyielding"

Zhenjiang Correspondence: Zhou Fohai, the Jiangsu Provincial Government Member and Director of the Education Department, was sworn into office at 8:00 AM on the 13th in the assembly hall of the Provincial Government. Wu Zhihui was sent by the Central Government as a representative supervisor. Gu Zhutong, a representative sent by the National Government's Executive Yuan, presented the official seal and delivered an address. Zhou's reply stated that his responsibilities as the Director of Education in Jiangsu Province are very important. He stated that the student movement is turbulent, funding is difficult, and the thoughts of the education sector are very complex. He stated that he is willing to do his best to do his part. He said that he is a party member and it is his duty to serve the party. He stated that he did not come to Jiangsu to be an official, but to do things. In the future, he is willing to shoulder the responsibility of Jiangsu's education with an unyielding and hardworking spirit. He said that if he cannot succeed, he will resign immediately and will not cling to his position.

CU Representatives Petition to Maintain Education Funding

More than thirty student representatives, including Jiang Mianju from National Central University, and six teachers, including Yang Gongda (representative of the president) and He Haoruo, petitioned in Zhenjiang at 2:00 PM on the 12th because the Executive Yuan had decided on August 20th of the 18th year of the Republic of China that 1.32 million yuan would be allocated annually by the Jiangsu Education Funding Management Office. Currently, 610,000 yuan is in arrears. The newly appointed Director of Education in Jiangsu, Zhou Fohai, proposed at a provincial committee meeting, due to the financial difficulties of Jiangsu Province, that the allocation of funds would be stopped starting in the 21st year of the Republic of China. The students are terrified and have made five demands:

1. Request that the Education Funding Management Office pay off the arrears.

2. Zhou Education Director's proposal to not pay from the 21st year onwards violates the Yuan's order.

3. That it be based on the State Council's proposal for permanent compliance and be maintained by the Jiangsu Education Funding Management Office.

4. Guarantee that there will be no arrears without reason.

5. Express sympathy for the school's difficulties, but oppose sacrificing NCU.

6. Express the difficulties of the school to the education community.

At the time, the Education Funding Management Office was in a meeting and agreed to allow a representative to attend as an observer. The representatives sent Huo Zhizhen to attend.

Jiangsu Provincial Middle School Principals' Letter of Advice to Students to Resume Classes (II)

We, the principals of the provincial schools, usually discuss and learn with you students, respecting each other. In terms of identity, we are teachers, and in terms of status, we are no less than fathers and brothers. As fathers and brothers, we should do our best to love you, and as teachers, we should take on the responsibility of guiding you. Now, for the sake of loving and guiding you students, we must give the following earnest advice:

First, the patriotism of young people is mostly pure and bright, which goes without saying. However, the true spirit of patriotism is like steam. It must be condensed, united, fulfilled, and strengthened in order to generate power and move forward. If it is used intentionally and released at any time, it may seem enthusiastic on the surface, but it is actually broad and loose and does not generate power. It cannot drive the engine and make it move forward rapidly. It can be said that Mencius said, "I am good at cultivating my magnanimous spirit. As for this spirit, it is most great and most strong. If it is nourished with integrity and without harm, it will fill the space between heaven and earth." The urgent task for you students is to cultivate and store your own magnanimous spirit, so that it is fulfilled and strong. Then, one becomes ten, ten becomes a thousand, a thousand becomes ten thousand, and even countless. Accumulate the countless magnanimous spirits of young people and transform them into a fulfilled, strong, most great and most strong force, which is hidden in a box and moved when the time comes. If it does not fly, it will fly to the sky. If it does not make a sound, it will shock the world. This is what it means.

Second, the foundation of saving the country lies in profound knowledge and moral principles. It is expected that one can study science diligently and invent bacteriology and silkworm disease science. France's increase in productivity is enough to compensate for war reparations. Edison of the United States, during the European War, devoted himself to inventions for military use, such as special shells, submarine telescopes, aircraft search methods, and submarine detectors, and finally defeated Germany, which had a world-shaking spirit. Recently, according to reports, our army and the Japanese army fought fiercely in Tianzhuangtai. The Japanese army used bombing aircraft to destroy the railway, preventing our armored vehicles from advancing and retreating freely, which resulted in setbacks. Our aircraft have often crashed in sea trials, resulting in broken bones and many deaths. How can we use them to fight? Such things show that students, for the future, must have the greatest effort, the most practical skills, and the newest inventions in order to talk about saving the country, resisting Japan, and overthrowing imperialism. Buried in research, desperately seeking new knowledge and new skills, and catching up with the world's culture is the time for students to strive.

Third, if the students resolve to save the country in the future, they must get rid of the bad habits of romantic, decadent, and lazy ways and replace them with the spirit of perseverance and hard work. According to our observations, among the bad habits of the students, laziness is the most deeply rooted and cannot be eradicated. They are usually afraid of studying hard, afraid of exercising, afraid of working, afraid of military training, and afraid of enduring hardship. It is the word laziness that harms them. Even in this wave of school closures, the number of those who are truly enthusiastic, righteous, unafraid of hardship, and engaged in saving the country is undoubtedly large. However, there are also many who take advantage of the opportunity to practice their hedonism and live freely. The word laziness harms young people and harms the country a lot. In the future, students must sharpen their minds, rise at the sound of the rooster, engage in sports in addition to their studies in order to train their bodies and cultivate their minds, intensify military training, truly regard themselves as soldiers, and practice enduring hardship and fighting, as Zeng Guofan said, "Knock out your teeth and swallow the blood." Only such people are worthy of saving the country and resisting Japan. Otherwise, if they speak of saving the country but only want to be comfortable, enjoy happiness, be a young master, and be greedy for petty gains, there is no such thing in the world. In short, having energy but no strength is not enough to save the country. Not learning and having no skills is not enough to save the country. Wanting to be free and comfortable and being unwilling to endure hardship is even more insufficient to save the country. Nurture your spirit and do not let it leak easily. Store your knowledge and strive to make it abundant. Exercise your body so that it can withstand wind, rain, frost, dew, hardship, and difficulty without fear or discouragement. The nation and the country will rely on it.

Hangzhou Association of Faculty and Staff from Secondary and Higher Education Institutions Established

The Hangzhou Association of Faculty and Staff from Secondary and Higher Education Institutions held its founding meeting yesterday afternoon at 3:00 PM in the public amusement park on the upper floor of the Provincial Public Education Hall. More than forty representatives from twenty schools attended. Yang Daoyuan was elected as the temporary chairman. After performing the necessary formalities, the chairman reported on the purpose of the meeting and the preparations. Then, the association's constitution was discussed and resolved. The name was decided to be the Hangzhou Temporary United Association of Faculty and Staff from Secondary and Higher Education Institutions (because more than ten faculty and staff from schools had not yet been able to participate due to school examinations, so the word "temporary" was added). All other articles were temporarily adopted, except that the number of directors was changed to seventeen and the membership fee will be amended at the next general meeting. The election of directors resulted in the election of seventeen people: Fang Zhichao, Xu Fangchu, Yang Daoyuan, Song Chongyi, Xiang Shiyuan, Shen Xianzhen, Zhu Husheng, Lu Dadao, Zhu Yiqing, Ye Hanzhang, Chen Chongran, Huang Shijin, Wang Zhenqiu, Luo Binren, Zhang Tingjie, Xing Xiping, and Yu Guozhen. There were fourteen proposals, but due to the lateness of the hour, it was resolved to hand them over to the board of directors.

Local News

Telegram of the Shanghai University Students' Union

Hoping that the National Public Will Automatically Organize to Overcome National Difficulties, the Shanghai University Students' Anti-Japanese National Salvation Federation sends a telegram saying: To the respected newspaper offices for public review by the national populace: Since September 18th, bad news has been frequently reported, causing alarm and repeated reports. All compatriots throughout the country are shocked and dismayed. The government bears the responsibility of defending the country and the heavy trust of the people. However, when the enemy comes, it does not resist; when the borders are threatened, it completely abandons them. During these hundred-plus days of national crisis, what has the government done? Apart from repeatedly declaring that it has final determination and measures, it only cries out to the League of Nations, demarcates Jinzhou as a neutral zone, and creates the idea of ​​joint management of Tianjin, causing a national sensation. Speaking of internal affairs, there is division and separation; speaking of diplomacy, there is loss of national sovereignty and power. It sings the high-sounding tune of serving the country and the people, but engages in actions that harm the country and the people. We, the young students, are in a state of danger and shock. Based on our patriotic sincerity, we have repeatedly petitioned the government to use force to resist Japan, and we are willing to be the backing. However, the government repeatedly uses the credibility of the League of Nations and the determination of the National Government as the only guarantee for recovering lost territory. It has not been adopted, and the patriotic movement has been wantonly destroyed. This time, students from various places went to Beijing to demonstrate, and their purpose was nothing more than to urge the government to unite and implement resistance against Japan. However, the government disregarded the students' enthusiasm, gave guidance and added reactionary labels, disregarded it brazenly, issued arrest orders, and inflicted beatings, with injuries and deaths along the way, and throwing them into the wilderness. We sincerely do not understand the government's intentions. Its high-handed methods dare not be applied to the enemy, but are applied to students who have no power. Alas, our young students failed to die gloriously on the battlefield of resisting Japan, but died unjustly in the dignified capital. Now that the national righteous debt unity has been promoted and achieved, and the new government has begun to realize it, pacifying internal affairs and resisting foreign aggression should be done to comfort the people's hopes. However, they are competing with each other to prove who is superior, forming a situation of division. The three gentlemen Hu, Wang, and Jiang have all indicated that they will go to Beijing. In the past, they monopolized dictatorship, but now they all stand idly by. Meanwhile, the violent Japanese have captured Jinzhou, and the foreign minister has changed twice, but there is still no policy toward Japan. The three northeastern provinces are almost completely lost, and they are now attacking Rehe in an attempt to seize Tianjin and Peiping, with a great tendency to annex the entire country. It seems that they are being slaughtered by others in this way, yet they are still humbly yielding. What is their intention? How can our compatriots not be wary and startled? The government cannot defend against insults and resist the enemy, and it even kills civilians and suppresses patriotic movements. The facts are there, and there is nothing to quibble about. For the sake of today's plan, if we want to save ourselves from danger and destruction, compatriots from all walks of life should unite and concentrate their will and strength. The violent Japanese can subdue our government, but they can never subdue our people. The government can cruelly kill young people, but it can never kill all young people. At this critical moment of survival, we hope that the national populace will automatically organize, overcome national difficulties together, recover lost territory, uphold the spirit of fearlessness, carry out the national salvation movement, and resolutely resist governments that harm the country and oppress the people. We sincerely hope that all sectors will unanimously advocate for early realization, drive out the Japanese pirates, and return our mountains and rivers. The telegram is not to be expected, respectfully, the Anti-Japanese National Salvation Federation of Shanghai University Students bowed respectfully.

Petition Situation of the Delegation of Middle School Students Going to Beijing

Petition to the Jiangsu Local Court

The representative, Zeng Guangchi, has been released

The delegation of middle school students going to Beijing to petition wired Xinsheng News Agency from the Executive Yuan in Beijing yesterday, reporting on the situation of petitioning for the release of the representative from Peiping, Zeng Guangchi, etc. The original telegram stated: On the afternoon of the 12th, at 2:00 PM, when they arrived at the gate of the Jiangning Local Court, the gatekeepers stopped them. After negotiations, they were granted access to the reception room, where they were received by the prosecutor. He said that Beida students must have a substantial guarantor to be released. This is a legal procedure and must be followed. Ms. Sun, the representative of the Peiping Anti-Japanese Association, offered an out-of-town guarantee. This delegation (i.e., the delegation of middle school students going to Beijing) immediately decided to return to the court in the name of this delegation to see the prosecutor, but they were denied access. The representatives strictly guarded each door, preventing people from entering and exiting, declaring that they would not leave the court unless the Beida students were released. At 12:00 midnight, the Peiping representative finally found a guarantor, but there were no responsible persons in the court. They searched separately and roused a judge from a bedroom, presented the guarantee, and then he agreed to release him. The five representatives waited quietly until 3:00 AM (13th). Beida student Zeng Guangchi was released from prison. Zeng wore a blue long gown and had a smile on his face. His hair was very long. In the court, he thanked the representatives, saying that he was grateful for their assistance and regained his freedom. He expressed his thanks and hoped that they would identify clear goals and work hard on the anti-Japanese cause in the future. Then, the students cheered and returned to the Executive Yuan. The Beida representative also stayed overnight at the Executive Yuan that evening. It was already 4:00 AM. On the night of the 13th, all thirteen released Beida students went to the Executive Yuan to express their gratitude. Ms. Sun, the representative of the Peiping Anti-Japanese Association, delivered a speech. They dispersed at 11:00 PM.

Jin Da Petitioning Students Arrive in Shanghai One After Another

Nanjing Jinling University students, after discussing abandoning classes, went to Shanghai and Hong Kong to urge Wang, Jiang, and Hu to go to Beijing to take charge of the government. Some arrived in Shanghai the day before yesterday, and more arrived last night, totaling more than 500. It is now known that they are temporarily residing at Jiaotong University in Xujiahui. Qingxin Girls' Middle School Resumption Dispute

The Middle School Federation Intervenes, Still Strikes Immediately

(Shanghai News Agency) The General Strike Picket Team of the Anti-Japanese National Salvation Federation of Middle School Students in this city, because a member school, Qingxin Girls' Middle School, violated the general strike agreement and resumed classes on its own, sent personnel to persuade them on the day, but to no avail. A misunderstanding occurred in the language between the two parties, and a slight conflict arose. After receiving the report, the team immediately convened a meeting and decided to take final measures. Yesterday afternoon, representatives were dispatched to lead hundreds of volunteer soldiers from more than a dozen schools to surround the school, and the situation was turbulent. They questioned the school's Anti-Japanese Association. Subsequently, the school sent four representatives to explain to the team's representatives, stating that the resumption of classes on their own was due to various difficulties. The two sides discussed for three hours, each sticking to their own opinions, and still could not resolve the issue. The situation was reported to Chief Jin of the Third Section of the First District of the Municipal Public Security Bureau, who feared causing trouble, and quickly took the police to mediate. As a result, the Qingxin Middle School representative agreed to temporarily suspend classes from tomorrow, and wrote to the Middle School Federation to request a general representative meeting to resolve the issue. The picket team felt satisfied and returned to the meeting at 4:00 PM to report.

Wang Jingwei Meets Representatives of Beijing and Hangzhou Students Yesterday

Sends Secretaries to Meet Separately, Indicates He Will Go to Beijing Once Recovered

Mr. Wang Jingwei is ill in the hospital and has been asked to rest. Therefore, he has not met with any guests. The Jinling University students from the provincial capital, who urged Wang, Jiang, and Hu to go to Beijing as a group, and the Hangzhou Federation of Higher Education Associations' petitioning delegation arrived in Shanghai from Beijing one after another to visit Wang's residence and urge him to go to Beijing to preside over the party and state's major offensive. Wang was unable to see them in person, so yesterday (the 14th) at 10:00 AM, he sent his secretary, Zeng Zhongming, to Jiaotong University to meet with the Jinling University students. At 3:00 PM, he sent his secretary, Peng Xuepei, to Shanghai Middle School to meet with the Hangzhou students, reporting that Wang would go to Beijing as soon as his illness improved, to live up to the wishes of the patriotic youth. The Jinling University students then went to Xujiahui Station at 1:00 PM in the afternoon to take a train to Hangzhou to urge Jiang. The Hangzhou middle school students also left Shanghai at 4:30 PM in the afternoon to go to urge Jiang.

Middle School Federation Petitions for Intensified Military Training for Students

The Anti-Japanese National Salvation Federation of Middle School Students in this city believes that the violent Japanese invasion is becoming more and more urgent, and the national situation is extremely critical, while the students' military training has become an ending, which is very painful. Yesterday, it specially petitioned the Training Supervisor Department to promptly urge all schools to intensify efforts to achieve results. The original state is recorded as follows: "To promote strict implementation of two hours of military training per day by the school authorities, today's foreign insults are approaching day by day, and the country is changing color. The Japanese pirates are deeply involved, and the country is dying day by day. Military training is urgent and cannot be delayed. Your department, in view of this, selects talents and sends them to various regions to be responsible for training, which is comforting. However, the training of various schools does not comply with the regulations of the clear orders, and it is perfunctory and sloppy. It lacks both the expression of spirit and the adequacy of time. There are often those who implement training and dismiss them in less than an hour. If this continues, how can it be effective, and how can it save the country? The responsibility of your department lies in this, and it should not be allowed to be corrupt without urging. Our Association is concerned and cannot sit idly by. I specially request your department to promptly urge the school authorities to strictly enforce the military training from the next semester and implement the two-hour regulation every day. Youth is fortunate, and the country is fortunate."
