Free Talk

Do Not Remove the Garden Grass, The Old Scholar Speaks

Thoughts on Reading the Declaration of Desperation of the Righteous Volunteer Army in Jinxi

A telegram from Shanhai Pass on the 10th said that the 6th, 7th, and 8th brigades of the Righteous Volunteer Army in Jinxi and the front-line junior officers of the Northeast Army jointly issued a declaration of desperation, which was sent to Yuguan by a special person from Honglu Mountain. The last paragraph of the declaration says:

"Our army is in the midst of the chaotic mountains around Jinxi and has entered the period of hand-to-hand combat with the Japanese. The intensity of their artillery fire and the number of our casualties are many times greater than those in the trenches of Dahuying. The number of enemies killed is also unprecedented. Knowing that the Japanese reinforcements have now encircled us in droves, our Righteous Volunteer Army and our defeated troops of the army have only a glimmer of hope and will never leave Jinzhou behind. We hope that the central government will quickly decide on a peace or war plan, and that the leaders of all parties will quickly put aside their struggles. If this is the case, even if our four thousand children in the Northeast are all martyred within a day or two, we should smile in the afterlife without regret..."

After reading this declaration dyed in the blood of four thousand righteous men in the Northeast, if we do not abandon our selfish views and go to the national crisis together, then we are truly heartless people.

These four thousand people do not have to die. If they are going to die, then they die for Rong Zhen, who retreated from the battle, for Zhang Xueliang, who did not resist, and for the central government, which talks about cooperation but does not go to the national crisis. They are going to die for their country, and this is their final question:

"Today we say cooperation:

Yesterday we said cooperation:

But there is no cooperation,

The Northeast is missing a corner!

The Northeast is missing a corner,

Cooperation or no cooperation?

Brother says unification,

If there is no unification,

Half of the country will be gone!

Half of the country will be gone,

Unification or no unification?"

Dragon Colt

— Swallow

In ancient times, King Mu of Zhou had eight steeds. They had the swiftness of chasing the wind and lightning. A Tang dynasty historical poem had a line that said, "The eight steeds travel 30,000 miles a day, why did King Mu have to come again?" This refers to this. When I was young, I liked to ride horses and test swords, and I galloped with the young men in the red dust and purple alleys to gamble for victory. At the same time, fast horses were popular at sea. One Thousand Red, Smoked Jujube, and Rolling Dragon of the Dong family in Huzhou were the most famous. Every time I rode alongside them, I could not catch up. I secretly sighed that the dragon colt mentioned in ancient times was probably like this. Qiao Zhucun, from Pu, is already seventy years old. He likes to talk about his youth. I occasionally chatted with him around the stove, and he told me about the dragon colt of the Red Goat Era. He had witnessed it flying. During the end of the Qing Dynasty and the Xianfeng period, the Taiping Rebellion disturbed Jiangsu and Zhejiang and occupied Jiangning. Only a corner of Shanghai in Jiangsu Province was protected by foreigners, leaving a piece of clean land. Xue Huan, the governor of Jiangsu, was stationed here. The various prefectures and counties without land gathered and relied on him. They spent their days chasing after his footmen and handbills. At that time, there was a certain prefect of Zhenjiang Prefecture, a banner man, who was a noble of the royal family. He kept dozens of horses. There were eight steeds in the stable, all of which had the reputation of traveling a thousand miles a day. Qiao heard about it and became curious. He went to see the horse. He only saw a horse tied to the trough, with miscellaneous hair. Its four hooves were like rafters. Its appearance was quite dull. He suspected that he had been deceived. He asked the groom, who said, "This is a dragon colt. If you don't believe me, please come and watch it in the early morning. You will be able to see its ability to fly." The next morning, Qiao went early in the morning to wait on the side of the gate. (The gate of the governor's office is the Yamen of the Daotai) Three or four horses were tied to the stone lions. The so-called dragon colt was also among them. Before long, he suddenly saw an official holding a command arrow and coming out. He climbed onto the saddle and mounted the horse. He walked slowly out of the West Gate. Qiao immediately called a messenger to ride a horse and follow him. By the time he reached the wilderness, he whipped his horse and galloped. He only saw the hooves flipping and dust rising. In an instant, he was gone. After a while, the sound of bells rang. The horse had already returned. According to him, he went to scout the traces of the bandits. It only took ten minutes to gallop dozens of miles. The cavalry of the Taiping bandits could not catch up. Its speed was like this. It can be seen that the title of dragon colt is indeed not a false reputation. It is a pity that there is no Bole in the world, and he was born at the wrong time.

The Phrase "Stacks of Bloodstained Clothes" Which Cannot Be Confirmed

— Yandang Student

Since the Northeast was invaded and occupied by the violent Japanese, student organizations have formed petition groups to ask the government to recover the lost territory and send troops immediately.

In addition to Peiping and Jinan, the petition groups are mostly composed of students from Shanghai. They went to Beijing in droves, with pure sincerity and indignant actions. They were forced to do so, not because they liked to be in power. Unfortunately, they clashed with the military police. It was not enough to stand out in the cold and snowy night all night. They were also subjected to prisoner abuse and sent to Xiaolingwei for placement. Moreover, rumors spread on the road that there were stacks of bloodstained clothes. The truth was half believed and half doubted, and there was no way to confirm it. Recently, I saw a poem made by a teacher of a certain school, which focused on the phrase "stacks of bloodstained clothes" which cannot be confirmed. I recorded it to introduce it to the readers. It is also a doubtful case in the voice of national disaster. The poem says: "The cold wind is rustling, the wind is fierce, the blood of ten thousand people is spraying on their chests. The youth are loyal and brave and die in vain. They do not die in the border city but die in the capital. They formed a team to petition to enter the capital. The rain and snow fell all night. The officials refused to see them. The valiant soldiers came to face the enemy. The bayonets were sharp and raised together. The unarmed youth all retreated. The painful words came and were shocking and doubtful. The stacks of bloodstained clothes were all crimson. If they fell into the water and died, they would still get a coffin. The fierce front destroyed them and it was difficult to find their corpses. The world should not have this kind of thing. Who can measure the shock and doubt? The strong enemies are gathering like hedgehogs in the Northeast. They snore and allow others to sleep on the couch. The anxiety is like burning to the youth. Who will fight and kill the thieves? Except for the hero General Ma, the rest have all disappeared and are hiding. The students petitioning are said to be out of position. The soldiers retreat and lose their jobs first. Alas, the youth are not afraid to die on the battlefield. Their corpses are not wrapped in horsehide. Are the stacks of bloodstained clothes true or false? I heard it as if the doubt could not be resolved. The soul is ethereal and cannot be summoned. If it is true, who will be cleared of the injustice?"

瀛海談屑

— 一臧

The Englishman, Mr. Lambert, who was an extraordinarily large man, has passed away. His weight reached over one thousand tons. He lived in Stamford. The circumference of his foot was more than three feet. The circumference of his waist was nine feet and four inches. He could sometimes jump to a height of over seven feet and often walked between London and Woolwich. He could also carry two adults on his back and swim in the water. Upon his death, he hired carpenters to make a large coffin for him, using elm wood that was one hundred and twelve feet long, six feet and four inches long, four feet and four inches wide, and two feet and four inches deep. Twenty porters carried this large coffin out of his house. When the coffin was placed on wheels, even the walls of the house shook and collapsed. Therefore, the road to the cemetery was specially constructed with a slope to facilitate the transportation of the coffin. He can truly be considered the largest man in world history.

A woman in London, England, broke the marriage record by marrying three hundred times. A single woman returning home stated that she had worn the new bridal gown used for marriage three hundred times. She is now displaying her wedding dress at the International Fashion Exposition to showcase its beauty. The wedding wreaths are almost like those in a flower shop. The number of bridesmaids hired for the weddings totaled the population of both London and York. She said, "I still wear fashionable wedding dresses because wearing them now is less awkward than when I got married. I used to love listening to wedding songs, but now I find them annoying. When I marry my three hundred and first husband in the future, I don't want to wear a wedding dress again and want to abolish rituals such as music and flower baskets."

關於巴黎最近藝壇的一封信（下）

— 劉抗

It is heard that in the near future, there are plans to first build a large building with studios, bedrooms, kitchens, etc., to accommodate impoverished artists at low cost or free of charge, to reduce their burden of living and allow them to focus on their research without any distractions. The goodness of this intention and the speed of its implementation are truly enviable!

Soon, a new Salon will appear. Its organizational principles are no different from others, but its purpose is different. The art displayed in this Salon will be based on the exchange of items or things that the exhibitors need or like, rather than money. It can be said to be a return to primitive bartering.

Next spring, a French landscape exhibition will be held at the Petit Palais, showcasing works from Corot to Cézanne. All the artists from the Barbizon school, such as Corot, Millet, Rousseau, Dupré, Diaz, Troyon, and Daubigny; realists like Courbet; Impressionists like Monet, Degas, Renoir, Sisley, Pissarro, and Guillaumin; and later artists like Cézanne, Gauguin, and Seurat will be represented. Efforts are being made to gather works from museums and major collectors around the world and exhibit them in one room. In 1925, there was a landscape exhibition from Poussin to Corot, which caused a sensation and attracted the attention of the general public and those engaged in providing for them. This time, the collection of works by realists and Impressionists, and the continuation of the study of nature from both scientific and anti-scientific perspectives, will be fully explored, making it extremely interesting. The grand occasion can be anticipated. However, I don't know if I will be able to feast my eyes on it, as my situation has become increasingly difficult and my finances have been severely hit. I may have to pack up and return home! If Mr. Hao's Lyon affair fails, I will set off to leave France in January or February of next year. I will purchase and collect A. Besnard's works when I enter the city and send them to you as soon as possible. When it comes to national affairs, everyone is disheartened. Military men and politicians exploit the people's wealth in peacetime and retreat and beg for mercy when something happens. This defeatist mentality is a great disgrace to our nation. If we want the Republic of China to stand in modern times, we must first revive the national spirit. Where does the national spirit reside? It is in literature and art. The master's vision is far-reaching, advocating the Chinese literary and artistic renaissance movement. I sincerely urge it to succeed!

黑白影展觀光記

— 苕狂

The Black and White Photography Society, organized by famous photographers such as Chen Chuanlin, Chen Zhude, Wu Zhongxing, Lu Shifu, and Nie Guangdi, specially gathered the works of its members at the beginning of this year, totaling 180 pieces, and held an exhibition on the third floor of the Times Building to promote the art. The exhibition was originally scheduled for three days but was extended for another day. I also took some time off during my vacation to visit and appreciate the works. I felt that there was one point that deserved special attention: the overall quality of the works was consistently high, with every piece exceeding the average level. This shows the concentration of talent in the society and the positive phenomenon of the popularization of photography today.

As far as my personal vision is concerned, I especially like the following pieces: (1) Wu Zhongxing's "Mad Crow," which is sparse, well-organized, and close to painting. (2) Fu Naowu's "Torrent," which is extremely surging and makes people feel awe-inspiring. (3) Chen Chuanlin's "Corner of the Racecourse," which embodies meticulousness in complexity and is clear at a glance. It shows that the artist knows the art of shrinking the earth. (4) Chen Zhude's "Ceiling," which is very much like a pattern painting and is truly ingenious. (5) Nie Guangdi's "Return Our Rivers and Mountains," which is innovative in its symbolism and shocking to the eye. I hope that my compatriots will be inspired by it. In addition, among the members, Dr. Lu Shifu's works are particularly numerous and worth appreciating, especially the "Maidservant," which has the meaning of a nude beauty painting.

It is also heard that, except for the items for sale, all the proceeds from the first sale of each exhibit will be donated to relieve the victims of the flood. Their eagerness to help those in need is commendable. (Thank you)

戎馬雙樓記（十）

— 求幸福齋主人

Chapter Two: A Heartbreaking Message Delivered to a Kind Teacher Amidst Laughter; A Home Devastated by Robbery, with Lonely Pity for a Friend; A Spring-Like Atmosphere in a Lodging with Delightful Conversation

Liang Xiaoyun, filled with joy, rushed to the door taking three steps as two, expecting to be visited by the high-achieving college student, An Yutian. However, instead of An Yutian, a man with a Japanese-style mustache, dressed in a Western suit, entered. It was clear that An Yutian did not look like this. After entering, the man heavily threw a thick foreign book he was holding onto the table with a loud thud, jolting Liang Xiaoyun's dreamy mind awake. She focused her eyes on the man and recognized him as the contracted English teacher, Wei Zhuomou. Wei Zhuomou was short in stature and very good at humor, somewhat resembling Charlie Chaplin. He was originally an English lecturer at the university, but due to his sociable nature, he met Liang Xiaoyun at a dance hall and became her private English tutor. Considering it a friendly favor, he was particularly diligent in this part-time job. Every day, between two and three in the afternoon, he would arrive on time regardless of the weather, never absent or late without a good reason, more diligent than his work at the university. Today, after entering and putting down the book, he immediately approached Liang Xiaoyun with a smile, shook her hand, and carefully examined her face and body. Then, with a heron-like smile, he asked, "Did you stay up late again last night? What did you do for entertainment? You don't seem very energetic today." Liang Xiaoyun smiled lazily, "Just those boring entertainments, making me feel so tired. I'm really getting tired of those meaningless social obligations." Wei Zhuomou continued to smile, "Since you're not feeling well, maybe we should skip today's English lesson?" Liang Xiaoyun thought for a moment and said, "I'd be bored anyway. We can just play around with a lesson." Wei Zhuomou quickly said, "That makes sense. We'll just play around. If you don't like it, we'll stop immediately. I'm a very polite teacher to my students. I'm afraid of annoying the students, or they'll cut off my job, and where else can I find such a good place and good student?" After speaking, he quickly picked up the foreign book, took two steps forward, and walked to a small door on the west side of the room. He bowed respectfully and gestured with his hand politely, saying, "Student Miss, please go to the study." Liang Xiaoyun couldn't help but cover her mouth and giggle at his actions. She glanced at the teacher and said, "What are you doing? How can a teacher be so mischievous with his student?" Wei Zhuomou still maintained his half-smiling, half-serious, comical face, bending over, waving his hand, and standing motionless by the door, not saying another word. Liang Xiaoyun couldn't resist him and could only sway her willow waist and lotus steps, laughing like a flower trembling wildly in the light breeze. She lowered her head and rushed into the study in the west wing. Wei Zhuomou followed behind in a serious and respectful manner, like a dutiful servant.

Commercial News

金融標金變動力大

Significant Fluctuations in Gold Bar Bidding

The market conditions were erratic, ultimately falling by four taels. The gold bar bidding yesterday fluctuated and fell, with significant volatility. The market shifted erratically, advancing and retreating without a fixed pattern. The daily difference amounted to fifteen or sixteen taels, a fluctuation not seen for many days. The final result was a drop of about four taels, leaving traders uncertain and erratic. It initially opened higher, reportedly due to falling silver market prices, subsequently reaching 690 taels. Later, foreign exchange turned negative, with more selling pressure, causing the gold price to depreciate by four or five taels. The selling pressure intensified, mainly due to the weakening of the US dollar. Dealers tended to sell, pushing the price from $13.4375 to $13.625. Consequently, market sentiment weakened, plunging below 80 taels. Eventually, the market seemed to stabilize as sellers rushed to cover their positions, leading the exchange to set a dual closing price.

Opening with a rise of five taels: The market opened five taels higher at 687.5 taels. The price of both large silver bars and US silver coins fell by one-eighth. It slightly increased by one tael to 86.4 taels. However, Yuan Li, Xie Xing, Yong Qian, Chang Xiang, Yi Feng, Yuan Mao, and others stepped in to buy. British gold settled at 11 pence and 25 points, while the US dollar was at $33.0625. India made purchases, causing the price to rise by three taels to 90 taels. However, HSBC and others offered March British gold at 25, and Zhifeng, Yongwu, and others sold, causing the price to drop by two taels. The posted price for British gold remained unchanged at around 88 taels. Before long, it rose to 88 taels and 8 qian. From 9:30 to 10:00, there was a brief lull. Subsequently, Fuchang, Zhifeng, Yongyu, Datong, and Taichang sold, but the foreign exchange market remained stable. By 10:30, it had fallen to 85.5 taels. Suddenly, Richang, Qianchangxiang, Yong Yuanmao, Yongfu, and others all entered the market. Taiwan also absorbed the April bonus of 1875, and San Kui offered 1875, purchased by Citibank, causing the gold price to rebound by three taels. At 10:50, it was at 8 taels and 6 qian. After 11:00, it showed signs of weakening. Mitsui offered recent US dollars at 25, and China Bank reciprocated with British gold at 3125. There were also many sellers in the market. Dadecheng, Zhifeng, Yongheng, Yuyu, and Fuchang all unloaded their holdings. By 11:30, it was at 84.3 taels. Afterwards, it increased by one tael. By the closing of the morning session, it had been suppressed to 4 taels and 6 qian, then moved up to within 3 taels, mainly due to physical goods being heavily sold off. The posted price was still calculated at 738.5 taels, an estimated turnover of 5455 taels.

Afternoon Market Turns Stable After a Decline: The market initially opened at 82.5 taels and subsequently dropped by more than 7 taels, indicating strong selling pressure. Richang, Qianchangxiang, Cuichang, Dingchang, Fuchang, and Yongyu all sold. Maihang first absorbed US dollars at $33.4375, followed by Zhenjin and Mitsui buying half a yuan. Maihang bought at $33.5625, reaching 75.5 taels by 2:20. At this point, Hengxing and Hongyong bought in, immediately pushing the price to 7 taels and 8 qian. However, with the US dollar weakening further, Mitsui offered April at $33.5 and then May at $13.625, coupled with Yuanmao, Xie Xingyong, Wanxing, and Shunli all offering, the final price at 2:30 was 74 taels and 4 qian. Market sentiment deteriorated. Shortly after, Maihang absorbed April at $33.5625, and Zhenjin absorbed March at $33.5. Additionally, Zhifengyong, Hengxing, Qianchangxiang, Runchangyu, and others all bought, pushing the price upwards. By 3:30, it was at 77 taels, 5 qian, and 9 qian. However, with retail sellers entering, it retreated to around 75 taels. At 4:00, a sudden advantage emerged as Fuyu, Yuanmao Yong, Heng Yu, Yuanda Yong, and others rushed to buy, pushing the price up by four taels in half an hour, reaching 78 taels, 6 qian, by the closing time of 4:30, a slight decrease of 3 taels and 9 qian compared to the previous day. Afterwards, it rallied by more than two taels to 80 taels, with Yuanmao Yong continuing to buy tirelessly. The daily high was 90 taels, and the low was 74 taels and 4 qian, a difference of 15 taels and 6 qian. Physical goods opened in the morning at 87 taels, closed at noon at 83 taels, and closed in the afternoon at 78.5 taels. The price difference was estimated at 60 taels. The accounts were settled at 87 taels and 85 taels in the morning and 81 taels and 79 taels in the afternoon. The water rate was 87 taels in the morning and 81 taels in the afternoon. Red strips were increased by 8.5 to 11 taels. Taikangrun made some purchases.

Traders Had Different Positions: Surface trading was still smooth. Statistics showed that Yuan Mao Yong, Yi Feng, Qian Chang Xiang, Xie Xing Yong, Ri Chang, Yi Feng Yong, Hong Kang Yong, and Yuan Mao all bought. 公債停拍後之滬金融界

Shanghai's Financial Circles After the Suspension of Public Bond Auctions

Funds from Various Regions Arrive in Shanghai, and the Money Market is Not Expected to Be Tight. The Principal and Interest on Treasury Bonds Will Be Paid as Scheduled at the End of the Month.

The recent changes in the financial world, due to the entanglement of public bonds, have often led to unfortunate incidents. A few days ago, the securities exchange was rumored to be suspending the right to auction due to the issue of various government authorities intercepting customs and salt tax revenues, causing a significant shock to the silver and money industries. The influx of silver dollars was indescribable. Subsequently, the industry devised methods to remedy the situation, allowing it to turn danger into safety. The following is a summary of the observations made. (1) The monthly principal and interest payments for various public bonds and securities amount to approximately 15 to 16 million silver dollars. There is a guaranteed amount of 6 million silver dollars that can be obtained on time. Banks plan to temporarily set aside 5 million silver dollars, leaving a shortfall of 3 to 4 million silver dollars. This will be supplemented by transfers from the salt surplus and related items. Therefore, the payment of interest and principal for this month can still be carried out as usual. (2) The financial industry has the closing period at the end of January of the lunar calendar, for the 20th year, for consolidating all transactions and accounts, resulting in strong capital. Even if unfortunate events occur, there is actually no panic. (3) In order to repay debts owed to Shanghai businesses, customers from various regions have been sending large quantities of cash to Shanghai. The available funds in the market are sufficient for distribution, avoiding the previous tight money situation. (4) Various stores outside are now implicitly suspending operations, making no funds available, so there are only surpluses, and no empty accounts. From this perspective, it is possible that the current major crisis will be safely overcome.

Yesterday, the financial market restored its former state, and a storm was averted.

Grains: Rice Market Transitions from Brisk Sales to Sluggishness

In southern Shanghai yesterday, the inventory of river rice remained high, with some supplies arriving. As the end of the lunar month is approaching, both parties are customarily settling accounts, resulting in quiet sales. Prices of various types of rice fluctuated slightly. Ordinary early glutinous rice fell by half a corner, while early rice [prices] were firm. Transactions of Luyang rice were scarce, also down by 5 fen. Arrivals of Tong grain decreased gradually, and the situation continues to weaken. There are approximately 70 boats in the river, each carrying an average of 110 shi of rice, totaling about 7,700 shi.

Transactions at Xinzha were not favorable. Arrivals of Changshu and northern rice were limited. Sand barges handled nearly 1,000 shi. Due to the approaching end of the lunar month, retail sales were limited. Over ten boats of [early] rice arrived, but market sales were active, and prices were close to one corner [per shi]. Arrivals of Jinlu late rice were very few, and the trend is firm. Inferior quality rice was a few fen lower. There was little change in foreign rice.

Spot Foreign Rice Sales Active

Futures Still Being Dumped by Foreign Firms

Yesterday's foreign rice market saw good sales locally, which attracted merchants to procure goods, resulting in an improved market. Flour Mills Keep Releasing Stocks

Yesterday's flour market saw prices turn weak and fall in the morning and afternoon sessions. In the morning, due to concerns about potential major changes in the domestic situation, many people rushed to sell their holdings, causing prices for all months to decline. By the afternoon session, the current month remained stable, but the forward months were impacted by the release of stocks by flour mills, although the quantity was not large. This caused prices to fall again slightly. Looking at the future trend, if the mills continue to release stocks, the market may have difficulty stabilizing. As a result, the current month fell by 12.5 fen compared to the previous day, February fell by 2.25 fen, March to May each fell by 1.7 fen, and June fell by 1.5 fen.

Wheat Market Fluctuates Greatly

Yesterday's wheat futures market saw prices slightly stabilize after the morning opening due to a rise of about one corner in foreign wheat quotes. However, trading was very quiet with minimal price fluctuations. Trading became more active in the afternoon opening, and the market was slightly affected by the renewed weakness in the flour market. However, selling was very limited, so the decline was limited. Observing the future trend, if there are no major changes in foreign wheat prices, the market may temporarily stabilize. As a result, January to March each rose by 1 fen, April was down by 1.5 fen, and May and June saw no change.

Local News

The National Crisis Relief Association Asks the Government to Decide on a Grand Plan

Recover Lost Territory

Return Political Power to the Entire People

The National Crisis Relief Association telegraphed all parties, stating: Chairman Lin of the Nanjing National Government, President Sun of the Executive Yuan, Vice President Chen, Minister He, Mr. Chiang Kai-shek of Fenghua, Mr. Wang Jingwei of Shanghai, Mr. Feng Huanzhang, Mr. Li Delin, Mr. Yan Baichuan of Taiyuan, Mr. You Zhantang of Guangzhou, Mr. Chen Bonan, Mr. Bai Jiansheng, Mr. Zhang Hanqing of Beiping, are all informed that recently, the brutal Japanese invaded Jinzhou and advanced deeply. Volunteer troops outside the customs have risen up to kill the enemy. The United States has also issued a serious protest. However, our defending troops retreated without a fight. National generals were suspicious and selfish. The so-called central government is even more elusive. You, as leaders of the party and the country, are scattered and complacent, treating [the situation] as if it were Qin and Yue. The dangerous signs of national subjugation are appearing all at once. What else is there to say? However, we, the people, for the sake of urgent public service and national salvation, must still offer the most sincere advice to you. The country is a public instrument for 400 million people. The Kuomintang promotes party rule, but it is definitely not willing to be subjugated. If, even today, you still believe that the entire responsibility for national salvation can be shouldered by one party, then please remove everything, immediately gather in the capital, take on the responsibility of national defense, unite the entire nation for total mobilization, and recover lost territory to prolong the life of the country. If there are still unspeakable secrets, or restrictions that prevent you from doing anything, then the party has clearly gone bankrupt and should immediately return political power to the entire people, convene a national conference, and create a government for national salvation, so that the entire nation can fight together. Facing imminent disaster, there is no room for hesitation. How will you decide on a grand plan to atone to the world? Please immediately demonstrate with facts. Otherwise, the people, in their grief and indignation, will not be willing to sit and die, and may adopt extraordinary measures to seek self-salvation and national salvation. The urgent telegram awaits your decision. The National Crisis Relief Association of the Republic of China [signed by]: Xiong Xiling, Ma Xiangbo, Zhang Binglin, Zhang Yilin, Zhu Qinglan, Zhao Fengchang, Wen Zongyao, Li Genyuan, Zhao Hengti, Cheng Zikai, Tao Jiayao, Peng Yunyi, Zhang Yaozeng, Xu Yuangao, Guo Chunsen, Shen Junru, Wang Yungong, Luo Jiaheng, Li Weilun, Zhu Qinglai, Jiang Qun, Zhang Kewei, Xu Kecheng, Chen Zemin, Jiang Hengyuan, Wu Shan, Qiu Fenling, Zhang Shizhao, Wang Shao, Zhou Huipu, Zhu Weiyue, Huang Wenzhong, Shen Tianxin, Zhu Duomin, Li Yukun, You Zhi, Zhao Shuyong, Wei Bozhen, Zhang, Xiao Jianbin, Wang Ningdu, Hu Zusun, Li Weicheng, Daonan, Zhang Zhaotong, Chen Dingyuan, Yang Chunruo, Zhang Xiaocen, Liu Yi, Wang Jiangao, Qiu Cong, Xiong Ren, Wang Jusun, Guo Zhijiang, Zuo Shunsheng, Yu Nanqiu, Li Zuohui, Song Yunhui, Xu Diaoxi, Zhu Shaowen, Fan Deguang, Zhao Zhengping, Huang Yanpei, Chu Fucheng, and others.

Zhang Ji and He Yingqin's Conversation After Returning to Shanghai

The Crux of the Situation Lies in Guangdong

Chiang Kai-shek Expresses Yearning for Unification

Zhang Ji, the President of the Legislative Yuan, and He Yingqin, the Minister of Military Affairs, previously received orders to go to Ningbo to urge Chiang Kai-shek to come to Nanjing and jointly plan national affairs. The two gentlemen returned to Shanghai from Ningbo on the Ningxing vessel at 5:00 AM yesterday. That evening, the two gentlemen released responsible statements and distributed them to various newspapers. The details are recorded below. Question: "What was the result of your trip to Fenghua to urge Mr. Chiang to go to Nanjing?" Answer: "We left Shanghai on the evening of the 11th and arrived in Fenghua on the 12th. We immediately went up the mountain to meet Mr. Chiang and explained the current national crisis, the increasingly pressing diplomatic and financial situation, and the desire of all parties for Mr. Chiang to go to Nanjing to take on difficult tasks. Mr. Chiang's attitude was very sincere, and he was also very anxious about national affairs. He stated that although he has resigned from his duties, his desire for unification against foreign [aggression] remains the same. He will definitely support whatever he can do. He hopes that Mr. Zhesheng and his colleagues in Ningbo will be able to endure any hardship and rescue the country from its difficulties. He also hopes that all parties will consider the current difficulties, implement the resolutions of the peace conference, and support the National Government to maintain this bud of unification. Only then can the national unity against [aggression] that the whole country seeks be truly realized. My personal resignation this time was for the sake of promoting unification. As long as the country is truly unified and the entire party is truly united, and my personal presence in Nanjing is no longer considered an obstacle to unification, then at any time, if the party and the country have a mission, I will not hesitate to go through fire and water." Question: "What are Mr. Zhang's views on the current situation?" Answer: "Over the years, I have deeply felt the necessity of unity for the party and the country. After the Mukden Incident, I felt even more that all comrades responsible for political affairs have a responsibility to actively solve the national crisis. This trip to Guangdong and participation in the Shanghai conference were all aimed at this goal. I have never advocated that anyone resign during the national crisis. Therefore, the Shanghai conference did not have a resolution asking Mr. Chiang to resign. However, the comrades in Guangdong insisted on this point, believing that a unified government could only be formed after Mr. Chiang resigned. Mr. Chiang, in view of this, did not want to hinder unification because of his personal reasons, so he resolutely resigned and tried his best to achieve it. However, even though he is out of office, he still encourages us to support the unified government. His upright attitude is admirable. As for Mr. Wang, he is currently recuperating in the hospital. Although I followed the doctor's advice and was unable to meet with him, I also firmly believe that he has the same determination to overcome the national crisis. At present, to solve the difficult problems of diplomacy and finance, there is only one way: to maintain unification. The unified government in Nanjing was organized in response to the wishes of the comrades in Guangdong, and most of the personnel were from Guangdong. Therefore, no matter what, the comrades in Guangdong should first show their support to show their sincerity in seeking unification. As long as the two Guangs abolish their free special organizations, hand over tax revenues, and return to the state before independence, then all parties will not rise up to emulate them. Progressing along this path, unification will be true in name and reality, and finance will not fall into despair, and diplomacy will also have a reasonable solution. When Mr. Wang and Mr. Chiang enter Nanjing at that time, there should be no problems. Therefore, I believe that the crux of the current situation, to put it bluntly, is not in Wang, nor in Chiang, but in Guangdong. I sincerely hope that the comrades in Guangdong will prioritize the overall situation of the party and the country, change their ways, and maintain unification. I especially hope that Mr. Hu Zhantang will bear the heavy responsibility of the party and the country and use his sincerity to move the comrades in the two Guangs to complete unification and unite to resist [aggression]. Otherwise, the overall situation of the country will be beyond repair. Therefore, Mr. Yu Youren's trip to Hong Kong is a crucial step in the current situation. I urge all comrades of the party and all compatriots of the country to recognize that the crux of the situation lies in Guangdong and should make every effort to promote the resolution of the Guangdong issue. The Nanjing government should also take full responsibility for resolving the semi-independent state of Guangdong, and must not create unnecessary complications and cause social panic. If necessary in the future, order me to go to Guangdong again, and I am willing to work for it." Question: "What are Mr. Jingzhi's feelings on the current situation?" (Mr. He replied) "At present, to solve the national crisis, the prerequisite is true unification. If unification is only in name, the country will be in even greater danger. Rumors of a nine-province joint defense, etc., as of now, I firmly believe that they are absolutely not true. I heard that Mr. Chiang had also telegraphed in a private capacity to inquire about whether it was true, saying that if the rumors were true, it would be no different from a transformation of the warlord era, which would be contrary to the country's desire. Currently, the state of withholding national taxes and division, if allowed to spread, will lead to the formation of a separatist situation. How can we resist foreign [aggression]? I hope that the people of the country will pay attention to this, promote the support of the central government by all parties, and complete true unification, so that national affairs can be solved."

Yesterday's Joint Meeting of All Sectors

Agriculture, Industry, Commerce, and Education Declared Meeting Adjourned

Various Groups Present at the Meeting Decided on Important Matters

Scheduled Citizens' Assembly for the 17th

In view of the fall of Jinzhou and the Japanese invaders' advance on Shanhaiguan, representatives of various sectors including agriculture, industry, commerce, and education in this city held a joint meeting at the city chamber of commerce at 2:00 PM yesterday to discuss countermeasures against Japanese aggression and for national salvation. Because the number of attendees was less than that required, the meeting was adjourned. Instead, the groups that attended the meeting convened automatically and decided on several important matters. The following is a report on each item:

Participating Groups: The groups that participated in the meeting were Shanghai Dockworkers' Anti-Japanese Association, Northeast Sojourners' Association in Shanghai, Taiwan Youth Anti-Japanese Association, Faculty of Law, Modern Middle School, Yangshupu Elementary School, China Public School, Shanghai Eastern District Elementary School Students' Anti-Japanese Association, Unemployed Workers' Anti-Japanese Association, Jiangnan College, Binding Workers' Union, Youth National Salvation Alliance, Various Universities' Delegation to the Northeastern Volunteer Army Headquarters, Rickshaw Pullers' Union, Xihe Yarn Factory Workers' Union, Women's National Salvation Alliance, Wensheng English Specialty School, Dongya Sports School, Shen Qi Anti-Japanese Association, Tongxing Yarn Factory Workers' Anti-Japanese Association, Chinese Students Association of Japan, Shanghai Middle School People's Anti-Japanese United Association, Fujian Various Groups Delegation, Aurora University, Shanghai Fine Arts School, and over 200 other groups, with over 300 representatives.

Temporary Alert: Sun Mou, the captain of the 6th Company of the Shanghai Municipal Police Bureau's Police Brigade, in order to maintain order and prevent any incidents due to the large number of groups attending the meeting, placed 30 armed police officers stationed at the City Chamber of Commerce on guard. The Chamber of Commerce's security team was also fully mobilized to prevent incidents.

Adjournment Declared: At 2:00 PM yesterday, the original plan was for five representatives from the Municipal Farmers' Association, five representatives from the General Labor Union, five representatives from the Municipal Chamber of Commerce, five representatives from the Anti-Japanese Joint Association of Various Universities, and five representatives from the Anti-Japanese Joint Association of Secondary Schools to hold a joint meeting. However, over 300 representatives from various groups attended the meeting. After an explanation by the representative of the Anti-Japanese Joint Association of Students, it was deemed ineffective. The number of people originally scheduled to join the joint meeting had not reached the required number. Therefore, the Anti-Japanese Joint Association of Major and Secondary Schools announced, "Today's joint meeting is adjourned due to the lack of the required number of attendees."

Continuing the Meeting: After the Anti-Japanese Associations of Major and Secondary School Students announced the adjournment, they immediately withdrew. The various groups that attended the meeting insisted on continuing to hold a joint meeting of Anti-Japanese groups from all sectors. The meeting was then held in the auditorium of the City Chamber of Commerce. The People's Anti-Japanese United Association of Jiaotong University and the Xihe Yarn Factory Workers' Union were elected as the presidium, and the Chinese Students Association of Japan was elected as the recording secretary. At that time, for the sake of caution, the People's Anti-Japanese Association, the Students Association of Japan, and other groups were designated as inspectors to check the qualifications of each representative and to seat the press reporters. Anyone who was not a representative was rejected.

Chairman's Report: Yuan Yiqun, the chairman of the presidium of the assembly and the chairman of the Jiaotong University's People's Anti-Japanese United Association, stated in his report that today's joint meeting of Anti-Japanese groups from all sectors is convened because the brutal Japanese have forcibly occupied our three northeastern provinces and are continuing to attack our country. Now that Jinzhou has fallen and Shanhaiguan is in danger, the government has no solution and is relying entirely on the people to unite and deal with Japanese imperialism. Therefore, please express your opinions as much as possible and jointly discuss concrete measures to save our country from its current crisis and ensure the survival of the Chinese nation.

Important Matters Decided: The various groups that attended the meeting decided on the following matters: (1) Oppose the government's sale of the three northeastern provinces and do not recognize any secret treaties or agreements. (2) Oppose the government's failure to support the Anti-Japanese movement and the massacre of Anti-Japanese people. (3) Auction confiscated Japanese goods to help striking workers and unemployed workers. (4) Use the power of the people to take over the Shanghai Anti-Japanese Association. (Method) Use the power of the people to take over during the Citizens' Assembly. (5) Various factories, schools, and other organizations should organize true volunteer armies, declare war on Japan, and send telegrams to various armies opposing treasonous officers. (6) The people should organize their own teams to inspect Japanese goods. (7) Punish the various members of the Fujian Provincial Government (Method) (A) Send telegrams to the whole country. (B) Organize a people's court. (C) Overthrow the running dogs. (8) The people should use force to prevent the partition of China and the arrival of the League of Nations Investigation Team. (9) Support the striking workers in various factories. (10) Publish warnings in newspapers to the five representatives of the Anti-Japanese Joint Association of Various Universities and punish them separately. (11) Unify national Anti-Japanese groups and concentrate the power of the people. (Resolution) Discuss further at the Citizens' Assembly. (12) Oppose the government's indiscriminate issuance of public bonds and secret diplomacy. (13) Schedule the Citizens' Assembly for the 17th, at 10:00 AM, at the Nanshi Public Sports Ground. (14) Organization of the Citizens' Assembly: (A) Presidium: Workers from the Shenxin No. 7 Factory, China Public School, Anti-Japanese Association of Various Universities, Anti-Japanese Association of Secondary School Students. (B) Commander-in-Chief. (C) Inspection Team. (D) First Aid Team. (E) Traffic Team. (15) Organize a preparatory committee for the Citizens' Assembly and actively proceed. (16) Starting from the 17th, implement a strike of classes, markets, work, taxes, posts, and drills.

Finance Minister Huang and Deputy Minister Lin Have Not Been at Their Offices Since Yesterday

Finance Deputy Minister Lin Kanghou Talks About the Reasons for Resigning

No Solution for Politics, No Solution for Finance

Finance Minister Huang Hanliang and Deputy Minister Lin Kanghou have not been at their office at the Shanghai office of the Finance Ministry since submitting their resignations. The reporter of the Xinsheng News Agency visited Deputy Minister Lin Kanghou at the Bankers Association yesterday afternoon and inquired about the reasons for the sudden resignation. He granted an interview and stated, "My resignation is because Minister Huang has already indicated his resignation, so I also resigned to express my joint advance and retreat. Also, at the Sun Residence meeting a few days ago, there was a proposal to suspend the payment of principal and interest on public bonds, which is contrary to my original intention of serving as the Finance Deputy Minister. Therefore, even if I were to serve in the future, I would feel that I have no way to face the people. Moreover, the central government's expenses require 18 million yuan per month. Traditionally, one-third of the funds are paid in cash each month, and the remainder is borrowed from banks with public bonds as collateral. The public bond fund issued from customs is then allocated to the banks in the following month. Each month, it is supported by the credibility of public bonds. If the payment of principal and interest on public bonds is suspended, there will be no solution in the future. Moreover, since the organization of the Special Committee has no legal basis, disputes will inevitably increase. How can politics be put on the right track? If politics is not on the right track, there will be no solution for finance. Therefore, if you want finance to have a solution in the future, you must first have a solution for politics. If there is a solution for politics, not only finance, but everything else can have a solution."

The Origin of the Rumor of Misappropriation of Bond Funds

Zhang Jingjiang and Zhang Qun Mediate

According to the National News Agency, yesterday, a certain gentleman familiar with the financial circles said that the monthly expenditure of the Nanjing National Government must be 22 million, of which 18 million is for military expenses, 4 million for party and government expenses, and in addition, there is also the principal and interest repayment of public bonds and treasury bills, which has not yet been included at 14 million per month. On the revenue side, after the unfortunate incident of interception of national taxes occurred in various places, only the customs duties and consolidated taxes of the Shanghai Jianghai Customs amounted to 7 million yuan per month. As for the issuance of financial public bonds, due to the extremely tight money supply, the end of the lunar year is approaching, and the paper currency is particularly inflated, it is not easy to issue. Therefore, the financial revenue has sharply decreased, and there is no way to reduce expenditure. The special committee for dealing with the difficult situation decided to misappropriate 14 million yuan per month used for the principal and interest repayment fund of bonds for military and political expenses. Therefore, Finance Minister Huang Hanliang resigned, and it is said that Chen Mingshu is internally appointed to succeed him. After hearing the news, the local silver and money industries and the 25 treasury bill custody fund committee were extremely panicked and have already expressed their firm opposition. Zhang Jingjiang, a member of the Central Committee, was also worried that this policy was not very appropriate. The day before yesterday afternoon, he tried to persuade Zhang Yuejun to mediate, and Zhang agreed to do his best to mediate.

Various Groups Continue to Strive to Deny Suspension of Public Bond Principal and Interest Payments

Since all sectors of this city heard the news that the government was suspending the payment of principal and interest on public bonds, the Municipal Chamber of Commerce, the Bondholders Association, and the Silver and Money Industry Association unanimously expressed their opposition, as reported in yesterday's newspaper. Yesterday, various groups continued to strive for this, which is recorded separately below:

Municipal Party Department

The Municipal Party Department telegraphed the Central Executive Committee, and the Municipal Party Department telegraphed the Nanjing Central Executive Committee yesterday, (title omitted) Since the completion of the Northern Expedition of our Party and the establishment of the capital in Jinling, there have been many troubles in all directions, and government expenditures have been stretched. Public bonds and treasury bills have been issued repeatedly to provide financial support. The amount of the levy is no less than 700 to 800 million. This is not because the financial resources of the people are sufficient and there is surplus capital to bear this, but because the public sentiment hopes for governance and hopes that our Party will be able to respect and stabilize the country and save the people from water and fire. Therefore, they do not hesitate to exhaust their meagre strength and strive to subscribe. This kind of experience is really a manifestation of the people's sincere support for our Party. Recalling the years of the Republic of China, from three to four years, Yuan Shikai issued only 24 million public bonds, and even apportioned them to each county, exhausting their efforts, only to barely reach the full amount. After our Party came to power, it continued to issue public bonds up to 700 to 800 million. If combined with those issued by the Northern Government, the total amount is almost more than 100 million. From this point alone, it can be proved that our country's public bonds have been popularized among the general public across the country, and the situation is definitely not comparable to that of the Republic of China in the years three to four. Therefore, the people regard public bonds not only as a kind of circulating securities on the market, but also as the same as farmland and real estate. Once the credit of the bonds is shaken, the people who rely on this movable property for their livelihood will inevitably lose their source of food and clothing. At this time, the bandits and communists are everywhere, and after the great famine of last year, most of the people have no land to cultivate and no business to operate. If the principal and interest of these hundreds of millions of bonds are suspended, then tens of millions more people who have no way to support themselves will inevitably be added, endangering the foundation of the country, which is unbearable to imagine. And the commercial market will lose this large number of securities for turnover and circulation, and it will inevitably collapse, and the phenomenon of unemployment of the four peoples will be compensated. Moreover, it is feared that the majority of the people will also suspect our Party, thinking that this kind of policy is going the same way as the Soviet Union's denial of all debts, but with different approaches. And the actual panic caused at that time may be no less than the phenomenon after the Soviet-Russian European War. At that time, although the Soviet Union's production declined and the ruble was equal to waste paper, there was no basis for foreign economic aggression in the country, so it could rely on its power to implement an economic system that it had obtained, and in a few years, its national strength was restored. If in our country, there is only one decline. Therefore, the suspension of the principal and interest of all public bonds may be a relief measure in other countries, but in our country, it is directly a way of suicide. The situation is different and cannot be compared. If the unified government really wants to shoulder the responsibility of internal stability and external resistance, it should inherit the doctrine of our Party, respect the public opinion of the people, and do its best to eliminate all obstacles to unification, so that finances can be stabilized and people's livelihood can be restored, and then it can be said to resist foreign insults. It is impossible to create extraneous branches, abandon food because of choking, and use the local government's interception of tax money as an excuse to come up with this inferior policy of misappropriating public bond funds and suspending principal and interest payments. If there is such a proposal, it is earnestly requested that your committee make every effort to stop it and prevent it from being realized, so as to appease the people's hearts and stabilize the foundation of the country. Foreign Dollar within Two Days

Since the news of the suspension of allocation of bond principal and interest payments came out, the hearts of the people in the city have been panicked. The previous day, the money industry association's market opened at 74 cents, and people still looked high. They held on until 11:00, and the price could not be settled. The market saw this situation and believed that this matter was of great importance. If measures were not taken urgently, the people's hearts would become more and more floating. Therefore, the money industry association asked the Central China and Communication Banks for instructions separately. As a result, Hu Mengjia, the general manager of Jiaotong Bank, first sold 720,000 standard oceans from Jiaotong Bank. Later, the Bank of China also continued to sell 1 million yuan of cash. After these two banks released 1.72 million yuan, the ocean market began to calm down, and the market price gradually recovered to 71 cents, 9 li and a half. Hu Mengjia, the general manager of Jiaotong Bank, also invited the leaders of the money industry the night before to discuss ways to maintain the market. It is said that the result of the consultation was that the silver and money industries decided to maintain the market and do their best to stabilize the people's hearts. Therefore, yesterday, the ocean market in the money industry market was gradually settled due to the maintenance of the China and Communication Banks the day before, and the circulation of cash was much more. The China and Communication Banks were also worried that the cash was too surging and the price of the ocean was too low, and they even had receipts to level the market.

Foreigners Form Bondholders Association

According to news from the consulate, the number of various stable public bond treasury bonds held by foreign merchants in our country is about 80 million. Now that the bondholders have heard that our authorities have implemented the suspension of public bond principal and interest payments, the bondholders have risen up to contact the consulates of their respective countries. At the same time, the consul negotiated with the General Taxation Department of the Customs, and the guarantee fund for public bond treasury bonds must comply with the public agreement conditions and must not be misappropriated for other purposes. On the one hand, the foreign bondholders have prepared everything and will establish a bondholders association immediately to take concerted action.

Financial Circles Discuss Financial Issues

The rumor about the suspension of public bond principal and interest payments has caused significant economic unrest in society. A reporter specifically interviewed a certain important person who is related to finance. According to him, after the proposal to suspend public bond principal and interest payments was raised, capitalists ran around to inform each other, as if a catastrophe was imminent. On the 13th, the silver and money industries held meetings one after another, and there was no result until the afternoon. Until the 13th, Zhang Jingjiang mediated, and on the one hand, the government declared to maintain the credit of public bonds. On the other hand, the silver and money industries first handled an advance payment of 5 million to cope with the government's current difficulties. When Song Ziwen handed over, there were still more than 800,000 customs payments. Up to now, after half a month, the tax revenue has also accumulated 2 million. The banking industry is willing to make this payment public to the government. On the one hand, they asked the new government to notify Guangzhou and also transfer 6 million to the central government. This intention has been telegraphed to Sun Ke Chen Mingshu.

Municipal Party Department Telegram Asks to Delay the Establishment of a Special Committee

No Legal Basis and No Justice

Yesterday, a Telegram Detailed Three Major Reasons

According to the National News Agency, the Municipal Party Department telegraphed the Central Executive Committee, saying: Nanjing Central Executive Committee Jian, The newspaper reported that because the three members of Wang Jianghu cannot enter Beijing immediately, it is proposed to set up a special committee in the Central Political Conference and appoint nine people to preside over it. It will be submitted to your meeting for resolution. It is deeply panicked. At this time of national crisis, the Central Political Conference should be convened quickly in order to preside over all the major plans of the party and the country. It is imperative. However, since there is an organization of the Central Political Conference, there is no need to set up a special committee again. It is not only legally unfounded, but also creates extraneous branches and puts a bed on top of a bed, and there is no need for it in justice. Will it be said that the three standing members cannot attend Beijing? On December 29, the Central Political Conference held the 300th meeting. Due to the fact that Chairman Yu Youren chaired the meeting, many important cases were discussed and the candidates for the ministers of the National Government were determined. At that time, the three standing members had never been in Beijing. It is known that the meeting of the Central Political Conference does not necessarily require the attendance of the three standing members before it can be held. Moreover, the standing members of the political conference are only the chairmen of the meeting, and they are completely different from the standing committee as an independent organization. Even without a standing member as the chairman, each member can also elect a chairman themselves. There are precedents, and it is not difficult to review them. This is one reason why a special committee should not be set up. The three members of Wang Jianghu are the leaders of the party and the country. We sincerely hope that they can enter the capital hand in hand and go to the national crisis together. However, since they cannot go to Beijing at the same time in fact, weighing the urgency, Member Wang is near at hand and should be ordered to enter the capital first. If one standing member attends the meeting, it can be convened. There is no need for the three standing members to attend at the same time before a meeting can be held. Today's problem is not in the system itself, but in whether each person can be responsible. If they are not responsible, then there are many branches and leaves, and although there are many organizations, it will not help. This is the second reason why a special committee should not be set up. In the past, during the First Plenary Session, three organizational principles were resolved for the political conference. The first article stated that "the Central Political Conference is organized by members of the Central Executive Committee and members of the Central Supervisory Committee." It can be seen that the original intention of the plenary session was to concentrate talents and be jointly responsible, so as to avoid a few people from monopolizing power and being solely responsible. Therefore, the second article stated that "three standing members are set up, and they take turns to be the chairman when the meeting is held," and the organization of the standing committee is not adopted. The previous and subsequent meanings can be explained to each other. Now, a special committee is suddenly organized by a very small number of nine people to exercise the functions of the political conference, which is obviously contrary to the previously set principles. Moreover, the principles set by the plenary meeting cannot be changed by a small number of members. This is the third reason why a special committee should not be set up. At that time, foreign troubles were imminent and the national crisis was deepening. It was still too late to unite against the insult. Member Jiang has already left to promote unity, and Member Hu should come to the national crisis together. If it is to people, then people have already left. If it is to things, then things are already urgent. Therefore, today, we can only urge the three members to go to Beijing to take office and open the political conference as soon as possible to preside over all the major plans for saving the country. Taking care of people and things, there is nothing better than this. The establishment of the special committee is neither legally founded nor justified. This kind of deformed organization should be temporarily delayed to avoid complications. Is it appropriate? Please decide. Shanghai Special City Executive Committee Knocked, cold,

Youth Suicide Squad Departs Last Night

Headed to Beijing First, Then to the Northeast

More than fifty members of the Shanghai Youth Volunteer Suicide Squad for National Salvation departed last night at 11:45 pm on a fast train to Beijing, en route to the Northeast. Many people from various public organizations saw them off. The details are as follows:

Organizational Structure: The squad consists of more than fifty members, with Ye Bin as the Executive Chairman. It is divided into five departments: General Affairs, Finance, Organization, Propaganda, and Training, as well as two committees: Economic and Disciplinary. Zhao Yaojin has been appointed as a rear area advisor to handle rear area affairs.

The Anti-Japanese National Salvation Suicide Squad of Japanese-owned yarn factories donated a "National Pioneer" cloth banner. Family Members' Persuasion: All members of the squad hold the purpose of sacrificing their lives to save the country, so no one withdrew at the last minute. Yesterday, Hua Xiang, a soldier from the Second Company of the First Battalion of the Anti-Japanese National Salvation Volunteer Army Independent Regiment, was persuaded by his brother-in-law, who had come from Wuxi, and exhorted with righteousness. However, Hua Xiang believed that sacrificing his life to save the country was paramount, and other matters could not be considered. He remained unmoved.

Departure Details: All squad members gathered at the North Station at around 1 pm. After roll call, they rested at the station and sent representatives to negotiate with the station about train tickets, but to no avail. Finally, they boarded the train and departed at 11:45 pm.

Travel Route: Ye Bin, Executive Chairman of the squad, said that after arriving in Beijing, the squad will first visit the Mausoleum on Purple Mountain. After crossing the Yangtze River, they will take a train to Xuzhou, then transfer to the Longhai Railway to Zhengzhou, and then take the Pinghan Railway to Beiping. They will then detour out of the Pass to join volunteer armies from various places outside the Pass to face the national crisis together.

Suicide Declaration: Since the September 18th National Humiliation Incident, the brutal Japanese have taken advantage of our country's disasters and, with their boundless desires, invaded our territory, massacred our compatriots, and implemented their Koreanization strategy to carry out their Manchurian-Mongolian policy. Our compatriots cried out for help but were helpless and waited for death. Our government respects peace and supports the League of Nations. However, the so-called League of Nations is merely a transitional organization of 20th-century human civilization and has no real power to judge right and wrong. Therefore, for several months, the League of Nations has been the League of Nations, and the brutal Japanese have been the brutal Japanese, and they still carry out their gangster tactics, invading and plundering, doing everything possible. Having occupied Liaoning and Heilongjiang, they now covet Pingjin. Countless of our compatriots have died tragically, and the country has not yet perished, but the butcher's knife has already been placed upon it. It is a laughingstock to friendly nations. How can this be tolerated? Although a single horse can be easily overthrown and a lone tree is hard to support, we feel the pain of the people and deeply believe that every citizen is responsible for the rise and fall of the nation. Therefore, we have gathered comrades in Shanghai to organize the Youth Volunteer Suicide Squad for Anti-Japanese National Salvation to follow in the footsteps of patriotic martyrs, vowing to use our blood and heads to resist Japan and save the country. We swear not to return alive until the Japanese invaders retreat. We are purely motivated by patriotism and have no party affiliation. As long as it is Chinese territory and the nation is being defended, no matter where the disaster occurs or who is attacked, we are determined to have no boundaries and are willing to be pioneers, preferring to be war ghosts rather than slaves of a fallen nation. The rise and fall of the nation depends on this action. All our youth, come enthusiastically!

Local News Two

Conspiracy for Wealth Results in Whole Family Suffering on Dung Boat

Information on Stolen Funds is Discovered

Leading to the Tragedy of Being Drowned

Lin Changgui, a dung boat owner in the Huangpu River in this city, was targeted for his wealth, resulting in his entire family being sunk into the river, drowning six people, including men, women, and children. The results of the investigation are detailed below.

Family Lives on Dung Boat: Lin Changgui, from Dongtai, was 42 years old. His wife, Lin Wang, was 36 years old and pregnant. Their eldest daughter, Tong Nu, was 15 years old. Their second son, Lin Bao, was 9 years old. Their youngest son, Lin Gen, was 7 years old. They also hired a boat partner, Gu Zhengyun, who was 28 years old. They owned a large dung boat with a Shanghai Municipal Finance Bureau license number of 20912, which was docked at the Guangxing Road pier in Shanghai, serving as their home.

Going to Fengjing to Collect Debts: Lin Changgui specialized in transporting fertilizer to Songjiang Fengjing and other places, traveling back and forth between Songjiang and Shanghai, making quite a profit. His younger brother, Lin Changyun, lived with him. There were debts of over 2,000 yuan owed to them in Fengjing. At the beginning of this year, Lin Changgui first sent his younger brother, Lin Changyun, to Fengjing to collect the debts, but he failed to collect them. Therefore, Lin Changgui loaded a boat of dung in Shanghai and went to Fengjing himself, with his whole family accompanying him on the boat. After unloading the dung, he went to various places to collect debts, and had collected about half of them.

Brother Said to Return First, Younger Brother Delayed: After Lin Changgui collected the debts, he could not abandon his business in Shanghai, so he sailed back on the morning of the 11th of this month. His younger brother, Lin Changyun, had other private matters, so he followed his brother later, returning to Shanghai by bus on the 12th.

Boat Unharmed, People Missing: After Lin Changyun arrived in Shanghai the day before yesterday, he went to the Guangxing Road pier, but did not see his brother's boat. He calculated that Fengjing to Shanghai was a smooth journey, and his brother should have arrived in Shanghai on the 11th. Why had he not arrived after two days? He felt anxious and uneasy, so he went north along the Huangpu River to search. He found an empty boat near Jungong Road and Dinghai Road, which was his brother's boat. However, there was no one on board and no belongings.

Concluded to be a Tragedy of Being Drowned: Lin Changyun knew that something had happened, so he reported it to the water police station. The station sent Detective Bellis and Chinese Detective Sun Agui to investigate. The result was that robbers had tracked them to this remote location and robbed them. They must have been acquaintances, so they tied them up and threw them into the river. This was a tragedy of being drowned.

Two Bodies Found in Gaoqiao: The detectives immediately reported back to the police station, which notified the Life Saving Bureau to pay attention to dredging. Yesterday, the Life Saving Bureau recovered a female body and a child's body in Gaoqiao. They were immediately taken to the South Bund pier and notified the water police station. Chinese Detective Sun Agui took Lin Changyun to identify them. One was his sister-in-law, Lin Wang, and the other was his niece, Lin Sai. However, a gold locket on Lin Bao's neck had been cut off. The police station has decided to report to the local court for an autopsy today, and to continue dredging for the remaining bodies and thoroughly investigate the case.

Appeal of Assassins of Zhao Announced

Original Verdict Revoked, Sentence Changed to Life Imprisonment

Xia Shaoen and Wang Jinshan, the two assassins who assassinated Zhao Tieqiao, the former director of the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company, were sentenced to death by the Shanghai court. It is now known that the Suzhou court held three hearings and carefully reviewed the reasons for the Shanghai court's death sentence, considering them insufficient. Therefore, the presiding judge of the Criminal Division, Hu Shan, announced in court the day before yesterday that the original verdict was revoked and the two defendants, Xia and Wang, were sentenced to life imprisonment. This official document was delivered to the Shanghai Special District Court at 3 pm yesterday.

Baofeng Steamboat Robbed on the Wusong Sea Yesterday

The Baofeng steamboat, which sailed from Chongming to Shanghai yesterday, carrying more than 400 passengers, was robbed by more than 30 pirates at around 10 am as it passed the sea off Wusongkou. The pirates rampaged on board for about an hour before leaving, satisfied with their loot. Many passengers were shot and injured, one of whom, a passenger surnamed Liu, died of his injuries. The steamboat arrived at Wusongkou at 3:30 pm. Because someone had died on board, the Western captain reported it to the harbor quarantine office, which sent personnel to inspect. It was also discovered that one person was infected with smallpox. The medical officer immediately ordered that the steamboat not be allowed to dock and that all passengers and crew must be vaccinated and given preventive injections before being allowed to disembark. In addition to reporting the incident to the authorities for investigation, the passengers on the steamboat, whose spirits had just recovered, were allowed to go home at around 6 pm. The losses of all passengers on board are still being investigated.
